data DistinctionRole : Set where
  first-distinction : DistinctionRole
  polarity         : DistinctionRole
  relation         : DistinctionRole
  closure          : DistinctionRole

role-of : GenesisID ‚Üí DistinctionRole
role-of D‚āÄ-id = first-distinction
role-of D‚āĀ-id = polarity
role-of D‚āā-id = relation
role-of D‚āÉ-id = closure

data DistinctionLevel : Set where
  object-level : DistinctionLevel
  meta-level   : DistinctionLevel

level-of : GenesisID ‚Üí DistinctionLevel
level-of D‚āÄ-id = object-level
level-of D‚āĀ-id = object-level  
level-of D‚āā-id = meta-level
level-of D‚āÉ-id = meta-level

is-level-mixed : GenesisPair ‚Üí Set
is-level-mixed p with level-of (pair-fst p) | level-of (pair-snd p)
... | object-level | meta-level = ‚ä§
... | meta-level | object-level = ‚ä§
... | _ | _ = ‚ä•

theorem-D‚āÄD‚āā-is-level-mixed : is-level-mixed pair-D‚āÄD‚āā
theorem-D‚āÄD‚āā-is-level-mixed = tt

theorem-D‚āÄD‚āĀ-not-level-mixed : ¬¨ (is-level-mixed pair-D‚āÄD‚āĀ)
theorem-D‚āÄD‚āĀ-not-level-mixed ()

data CanonicalCaptures : GenesisID ‚Üí GenesisPair ‚Üí Set where
  can-D‚āÄ-self : CanonicalCaptures D‚āÄ-id pair-D‚āÄD‚āÄ
  
  can-D‚āĀ-self : CanonicalCaptures D‚āĀ-id pair-D‚āĀD‚āĀ
  can-D‚āĀ-D‚āÄ   : CanonicalCaptures D‚āĀ-id pair-D‚āĀD‚āÄ
  
  can-D‚āā-def  : CanonicalCaptures D‚āā-id pair-D‚āÄD‚āĀ
  can-D‚āā-self : CanonicalCaptures D‚āā-id pair-D‚āāD‚āā
  can-D‚āā-D‚āĀ   : CanonicalCaptures D‚āā-id pair-D‚āāD‚āĀ

theorem-canonical-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā : (d : GenesisID) ‚Üí ¬¨ (CanonicalCaptures d pair-D‚āÄD‚āā)
theorem-canonical-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā D‚āÄ-id ()
theorem-canonical-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā D‚āĀ-id ()
theorem-canonical-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā D‚āā-id ()

record CapturesCanonicityProof : Set where
  field
    proof-D‚āā-captures-D‚āÄD‚āĀ : Captures D‚āā-id pair-D‚āÄD‚āĀ
    proof-D‚āÄD‚āā-level-mixed : is-level-mixed pair-D‚āÄD‚āā
    proof-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā  : (d : GenesisID) ‚Üí ¬¨ (CanonicalCaptures d pair-D‚āÄD‚āā)

theorem-captures-is-canonical : CapturesCanonicityProof
theorem-captures-is-canonical = record
  { proof-D‚āā-captures-D‚āÄD‚āĀ = D‚āā-captures-D‚āÄD‚āĀ
  ; proof-D‚āÄD‚āā-level-mixed = theorem-D‚āÄD‚āā-is-level-mixed
  ; proof-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā = theorem-canonical-no-capture-D‚āÄD‚āā
  }


-- ¬ß ARITHMETIC

data _‚Č§_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set where
  z‚Č§n : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí zero ‚Č§ n
  s‚Č§s : ‚ąÄ {m n} ‚Üí m ‚Č§ n ‚Üí suc m ‚Č§ suc n

‚Č§-refl : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí n ‚Č§ n
‚Č§-refl {zero}  = z‚Č§n
‚Č§-refl {suc n} = s‚Č§s ‚Č§-refl

‚Č§-step : ‚ąÄ {m n} ‚Üí m ‚Č§ n ‚Üí m ‚Č§ suc n
‚Č§-step z‚Č§n = z‚Č§n
‚Č§-step (s‚Č§s p) = s‚Č§s (‚Č§-step p)

infix 4 _‚Č•_
_‚Č•_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set
m ‚Č• n = n ‚Č§ m

infix 4 _<_
_<_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set
m < n = suc m ‚Č§ n

infix 4 _>_
_>_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set
m > n = n < m

max : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
max zero  n     = n
max (suc m) zero  = suc m
max (suc m) (suc n) = suc (max m n)

min : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
min zero  _     = zero
min _     zero  = zero
min (suc m) (suc n) = suc (min m n)

[_] : {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí List A
[ x ] = x ‚ą∑ []

record ‚Ą§ : Set where
  constructor mk‚Ą§
  field
    pos : ‚Ąē
    neg : ‚Ąē

_‚ČÉ‚Ą§_ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí Set
mk‚Ą§ a b ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ c d = (a + d) ‚Č° (c + b)

infix 4 _‚ČÉ‚Ą§_

0‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§
0‚Ą§ = mk‚Ą§ zero zero

1‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§
1‚Ą§ = mk‚Ą§ (suc zero) zero

-1‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§
-1‚Ą§ = mk‚Ą§ zero (suc zero)

infixl 6 _+‚Ą§_
_+‚Ą§_ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
mk‚Ą§ a b +‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ c d = mk‚Ą§ (a + c) (b + d)

infixl 7 _*‚Ą§_
_*‚Ą§_ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
mk‚Ą§ a b *‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ c d = mk‚Ą§ ((a * c) + (b * d)) ((a * d) + (b * c))

neg‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
neg‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ a b) = mk‚Ą§ b a

‚ČÉ‚Ą§-refl : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
‚ČÉ‚Ą§-refl (mk‚Ą§ a b) = refl

‚ČÉ‚Ą§-sym : ‚ąÄ {x y : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí y ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
‚ČÉ‚Ą§-sym {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} eq = sym eq

normalize‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
normalize‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ a       zero)    = mk‚Ą§ a zero
normalize‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ zero    b)       = mk‚Ą§ zero b
normalize‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ (suc a) (suc b)) = normalize‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ a b)

theorem-normalize-sum-zero : normalize‚Ą§ (1‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ -1‚Ą§) ‚Č° 0‚Ą§
theorem-normalize-sum-zero = refl

theorem-normalize-2-minus-1 : normalize‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ 2 1) ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-normalize-2-minus-1 = refl

‚Ą§-trans-helper : ‚ąÄ (a b c d e f : ‚Ąē)
               ‚Üí (a + d) ‚Č° (c + b)
               ‚Üí (c + f) ‚Č° (e + d)
               ‚Üí (a + f) ‚Č° (e + b)
‚Ą§-trans-helper a b c d e f p q =
  let
    step1 : ((a + d) + f) ‚Č° ((c + b) + f)
    step1 = cong (_+ f) p
    
    step2 : ((a + d) + f) ‚Č° (a + (d + f))
    step2 = +-assoc a d f
    
    step3 : ((c + b) + f) ‚Č° (c + (b + f))
    step3 = +-assoc c b f
    
    step4 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° (c + (b + f))
    step4 = trans (sym step2) (trans step1 step3)
    

    step5 : ((c + f) + b) ‚Č° ((e + d) + b)
    step5 = cong (_+ b) q
    
    step6 : ((c + f) + b) ‚Č° (c + (f + b))
    step6 = +-assoc c f b
    
    step7 : (b + f) ‚Č° (f + b)
    step7 = +-comm b f
    
    step8 : (c + (b + f)) ‚Č° (c + (f + b))
    step8 = cong (c +_) step7
    
    step9 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° (c + (f + b))
    step9 = trans step4 step8
    
    step10 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° ((c + f) + b)
    step10 = trans step9 (sym step6)
    
    step11 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° ((e + d) + b)
    step11 = trans step10 step5
    
    step12 : ((e + d) + b) ‚Č° (e + (d + b))
    step12 = +-assoc e d b
    
    step13 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° (e + (d + b))
    step13 = trans step11 step12
    

    step14a : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° (a + (f + d))
    step14a = cong (a +_) (+-comm d f)
    step14b : (a + (f + d)) ‚Č° ((a + f) + d)
    step14b = sym (+-assoc a f d)
    step14 : (a + (d + f)) ‚Č° ((a + f) + d)
    step14 = trans step14a step14b
    
    step15a : (e + (d + b)) ‚Č° (e + (b + d))
    step15a = cong (e +_) (+-comm d b)
    step15b : (e + (b + d)) ‚Č° ((e + b) + d)
    step15b = sym (+-assoc e b d)
    step15 : (e + (d + b)) ‚Č° ((e + b) + d)
    step15 = trans step15a step15b
    
    step16 : ((a + f) + d) ‚Č° ((e + b) + d)
    step16 = trans (sym step14) (trans step13 step15)
    
  in +-cancel ≥ (a + f) (e + b) d step16

‚ČÉ‚Ą§-trans : ‚ąÄ {x y z : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí y ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ z ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ z
‚ČÉ‚Ą§-trans {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} {mk‚Ą§ e f} = ‚Ą§-trans-helper a b c d e f

‚Č°‚Üí‚ČÉ‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {x y : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚Č° y ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y
‚Č°‚Üí‚ČÉ‚Ą§ {x} refl = ‚ČÉ‚Ą§-refl x

*-zero ≥ : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (n * zero) ‚Č° zero
*-zero ≥ zero    = refl
*-zero ≥ (suc n) = *-zero ≥ n

*-zeroň° : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (zero * n) ‚Č° zero
*-zeroň° n = refl

*-identityň° : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (suc zero * n) ‚Č° n
*-identityň° n = +-identity ≥ n

*-identity ≥ : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (n * suc zero) ‚Č° n
*-identity ≥ zero = refl
*-identity ≥ (suc n) = cong suc (*-identity ≥ n)

*-distrib ≥-+ : ‚ąÄ (a b c : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí ((a + b) * c) ‚Č° ((a * c) + (b * c))
*-distrib ≥-+ zero    b c = refl
*-distrib ≥-+ (suc a) b c = 
  trans (cong (c +_) (*-distrib ≥-+ a b c)) 
        (sym (+-assoc c (a * c) (b * c)))

*-suc ≥ : ‚ąÄ (m n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (m * suc n) ‚Č° (m + (m * n))
*-suc ≥ zero    n = refl
*-suc ≥ (suc m) n = cong suc (trans (cong (n +_) (*-suc ≥ m n))
                     (trans (sym (+-assoc n m (m * n)))
                     (trans (cong (_+ (m * n)) (+-comm n m))
                     (+-assoc m n (m * n)))))

*-comm : ‚ąÄ (m n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (m * n) ‚Č° (n * m)
*-comm zero    n = sym (*-zero ≥ n)
*-comm (suc m) n = trans (cong (n +_) (*-comm m n)) (sym (*-suc ≥ n m))

*-assoc : ‚ąÄ (a b c : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (a * (b * c)) ‚Č° ((a * b) * c)
*-assoc zero b c = refl
*-assoc (suc a) b c = 
  trans (cong (b * c +_) (*-assoc a b c)) (sym (*-distrib ≥-+ b (a * b) c))

*-distribň°-+ : ‚ąÄ (a b c : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (a * (b + c)) ‚Č° ((a * b) + (a * c))
*-distribň°-+ a b c = 
  trans (*-comm a (b + c))
        (trans (*-distrib ≥-+ b c a)
               (cong‚āā _+_ (*-comm b a) (*-comm c a)))

+‚Ą§-cong : ‚ąÄ {x y z w : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí z ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ w ‚Üí (x +‚Ą§ z) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (y +‚Ą§ w)
+‚Ą§-cong {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} {mk‚Ą§ e f} {mk‚Ą§ g h} ad‚Č°cb eh‚Č°gf =
  let
    step1 : ((a + e) + (d + h)) ‚Č° ((a + d) + (e + h))
    step1 = trans (+-assoc a e (d + h)) 
            (trans (cong (a +_) (trans (sym (+-assoc e d h)) 
                   (trans (cong (_+ h) (+-comm e d)) (+-assoc d e h))))
            (sym (+-assoc a d (e + h))))
    
    step2 : ((a + d) + (e + h)) ‚Č° ((c + b) + (g + f))
    step2 = cong‚āā _+_ ad‚Č°cb eh‚Č°gf
    
    step3 : ((c + b) + (g + f)) ‚Č° ((c + g) + (b + f))
    step3 = trans (+-assoc c b (g + f))
            (trans (cong (c +_) (trans (sym (+-assoc b g f))
                   (trans (cong (_+ f) (+-comm b g)) (+-assoc g b f))))
            (sym (+-assoc c g (b + f))))
  in trans step1 (trans step2 step3)

+-rearrange-4 : ‚ąÄ (a b c d : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí ((a + b) + (c + d)) ‚Č° ((a + c) + (b + d))
+-rearrange-4 a b c d =
  trans (trans (trans (trans (sym (+-assoc (a + b) c d))
                             (cong (_+ d) (+-assoc a b c)))
                      (cong (_+ d) (cong (a +_) (+-comm b c))))
                (cong (_+ d) (sym (+-assoc a c b))))
        (+-assoc (a + c) b d)

+-rearrange-4-alt : ‚ąÄ (a b c d : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí ((a + b) + (c + d)) ‚Č° ((a + d) + (c + b))
+-rearrange-4-alt a b c d =
  trans (cong ((a + b) +_) (+-comm c d))
        (trans (trans (trans (trans (trans (sym (+-assoc (a + b) d c))
                                            (cong (_+ c) (+-assoc a b d)))
                                     (cong (_+ c) (cong (a +_) (+-comm b d))))
                              (cong (_+ c) (sym (+-assoc a d b))))
                       (+-assoc (a + d) b c))
               (cong ((a + d) +_) (+-comm b c)))

‚äó-cong-left : ‚ąÄ {a b c d : ‚Ąē} (e f : ‚Ąē)
            ‚Üí (a + d) ‚Č° (c + b)
            ‚Üí ((a * e + b * f) + (c * f + d * e)) ‚Č° ((c * e + d * f) + (a * f + b * e))
‚äó-cong-left {a} {b} {c} {d} e f ad‚Č°cb =
  let ae+de‚Č°ce+be : (a * e + d * e) ‚Č° (c * e + b * e)
      ae+de‚Č°ce+be = trans (sym (*-distrib ≥-+ a d e)) 
                          (trans (cong (_* e) ad‚Č°cb) 
                                 (*-distrib ≥-+ c b e))
      af+df‚Č°cf+bf : (a * f + d * f) ‚Č° (c * f + b * f)
      af+df‚Č°cf+bf = trans (sym (*-distrib ≥-+ a d f))
                          (trans (cong (_* f) ad‚Č°cb)
                                 (*-distrib ≥-+ c b f))
  in trans (+-rearrange-4-alt (a * e) (b * f) (c * f) (d * e))
           (trans (cong‚āā _+_ ae+de‚Č°ce+be (sym af+df‚Č°cf+bf))
                  (+-rearrange-4-alt (c * e) (b * e) (a * f) (d * f)))

‚äó-cong-right : ‚ąÄ (a b : ‚Ąē) {e f g h : ‚Ąē}
             ‚Üí (e + h) ‚Č° (g + f)
             ‚Üí ((a * e + b * f) + (a * h + b * g)) ‚Č° ((a * g + b * h) + (a * f + b * e))
‚äó-cong-right a b {e} {f} {g} {h} eh‚Č°gf =
  let ae+ah‚Č°ag+af : (a * e + a * h) ‚Č° (a * g + a * f)
      ae+ah‚Č°ag+af = trans (sym (*-distribň°-+ a e h))
                          (trans (cong (a *_) eh‚Č°gf)
                                 (*-distribň°-+ a g f))
      be+bh‚Č°bg+bf : (b * e + b * h) ‚Č° (b * g + b * f)
      be+bh‚Č°bg+bf = trans (sym (*-distribň°-+ b e h))
                          (trans (cong (b *_) eh‚Č°gf)
                                 (*-distribň°-+ b g f))
      bf+bg‚Č°be+bh : (b * f + b * g) ‚Č° (b * e + b * h)
      bf+bg‚Č°be+bh = trans (+-comm (b * f) (b * g)) (sym be+bh‚Č°bg+bf)
  in trans (+-rearrange-4 (a * e) (b * f) (a * h) (b * g))
           (trans (cong‚āā _+_ ae+ah‚Č°ag+af bf+bg‚Č°be+bh)
                  (trans (cong ((a * g + a * f) +_) (+-comm (b * e) (b * h)))
                         (sym (+-rearrange-4 (a * g) (b * h) (a * f) (b * e)))))

~‚Ą§-trans : ‚ąÄ {a b c d e f : ‚Ąē} ‚Üí (a + d) ‚Č° (c + b) ‚Üí (c + f) ‚Č° (e + d) ‚Üí (a + f) ‚Č° (e + b)
~‚Ą§-trans {a} {b} {c} {d} {e} {f} = ‚Ą§-trans-helper a b c d e f

*‚Ą§-cong : ‚ąÄ {x y z w : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí z ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ w ‚Üí (x *‚Ą§ z) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (y *‚Ą§ w)
*‚Ą§-cong {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} {mk‚Ą§ e f} {mk‚Ą§ g h} ad‚Č°cb eh‚Č°gf =
  ~‚Ą§-trans {a * e + b * f} {a * f + b * e}
           {c * e + d * f} {c * f + d * e}
           {c * g + d * h} {c * h + d * g}
           (‚äó-cong-left {a} {b} {c} {d} e f ad‚Č°cb)
           (‚äó-cong-right c d {e} {f} {g} {h} eh‚Č°gf)

*‚Ą§-cong-r : ‚ąÄ (z : ‚Ą§) {x y : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí (z *‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (z *‚Ą§ y)
*‚Ą§-cong-r z {x} {y} eq = *‚Ą§-cong {z} {z} {x} {y} (‚ČÉ‚Ą§-refl z) eq

*‚Ą§-zeroň° : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (0‚Ą§ *‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
*‚Ą§-zeroň° (mk‚Ą§ a b) = refl

*‚Ą§-zero ≥ : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x *‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
*‚Ą§-zero ≥ (mk‚Ą§ a b) = 
  trans (+-identity ≥ (a * 0 + b * 0)) refl

+‚Ą§-inverse ≥ : (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
+‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (mk‚Ą§ a b) = trans (+-identity ≥ (a + b)) (+-comm a b)

+‚Ą§-inverseň° : (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (neg‚Ą§ x +‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
+‚Ą§-inverseň° (mk‚Ą§ a b) = trans (+-identity ≥ (b + a)) (+-comm b a)

+‚Ą§-neg‚Ą§-cancel : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
+‚Ą§-neg‚Ą§-cancel (mk‚Ą§ a b) = trans (+-identity ≥ (a + b)) (+-comm a b)

neg‚Ą§-cong : ‚ąÄ {x y : ‚Ą§} ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y ‚Üí neg‚Ą§ x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ y
neg‚Ą§-cong {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} eq = 
  trans (+-comm b c) (trans (sym eq) (+-comm a d))

+‚Ą§-comm : ‚ąÄ (x y : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x +‚Ą§ y) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (y +‚Ą§ x)
+‚Ą§-comm (mk‚Ą§ a b) (mk‚Ą§ c d) = 
  cong‚āā _+_ (+-comm a c) (+-comm d b)

+‚Ą§-identityň° : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (0‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
+‚Ą§-identityň° (mk‚Ą§ a b) = refl

+‚Ą§-identity ≥ : ‚ąÄ (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x +‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
+‚Ą§-identity ≥ (mk‚Ą§ a b) = cong‚āā _+_ (+-identity ≥ a) (sym (+-identity ≥ b))

+‚Ą§-assoc : (x y z : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí ((x +‚Ą§ y) +‚Ą§ z) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (x +‚Ą§ (y +‚Ą§ z))
+‚Ą§-assoc (mk‚Ą§ a b) (mk‚Ą§ c d) (mk‚Ą§ e f) = 
  let
    lhs = ((a + c) + e) + (b + (d + f))
    rhs = (a + (c + e)) + ((b + d) + f)
    
    step1 : lhs ‚Č° (a + (c + e)) + (b + (d + f))
    step1 = cong (őĽ x ‚Üí x + (b + (d + f))) (+-assoc a c e)
    
    step2 : (a + (c + e)) + (b + (d + f)) ‚Č° rhs
    step2 = cong (őĽ x ‚Üí (a + (c + e)) + x) (sym (+-assoc b d f))
    
  in trans step1 step2

*‚Ą§-identityň° : (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (1‚Ą§ *‚Ą§ x) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
*‚Ą§-identityň° (mk‚Ą§ a b) = 
  let lhs-pos = (suc zero * a + zero * b)
      lhs-neg = (suc zero * b + zero * a)
      step1 : lhs-pos + b ‚Č° (a + zero) + b
      step1 = cong (őĽ x ‚Üí x + b) (+-identity ≥ (a + zero * a))
      step2 : (a + zero) + b ‚Č° a + b
      step2 = cong (őĽ x ‚Üí x + b) (+-identity ≥ a)
      step3 : a + b ‚Č° a + (b + zero)
      step3 = sym (cong (a +_) (+-identity ≥ b))
      step4 : a + (b + zero) ‚Č° a + lhs-neg
      step4 = sym (cong (a +_) (+-identity ≥ (b + zero * b)))
  in trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4))

*‚Ą§-identity ≥ : (x : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí (x *‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ x
*‚Ą§-identity ≥ (mk‚Ą§ a b) = 
  let p = a * suc zero + b * zero
      n = a * zero + b * suc zero
      p‚Č°a : p ‚Č° a
      p‚Č°a = trans (cong‚āā _+_ (*-identity ≥ a) (*-zero ≥ b)) (+-identity ≥ a)
      n‚Č°b : n ‚Č° b
      n‚Č°b = trans (cong‚āā _+_ (*-zero ≥ a) (*-identity ≥ b)) refl
      lhs : p + b ‚Č° a + b
      lhs = cong (őĽ x ‚Üí x + b) p‚Č°a
      rhs : a + n ‚Č° a + b
      rhs = cong (a +_) n‚Č°b
  in trans lhs (sym rhs)

*‚Ą§-distribň°-+‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí (x *‚Ą§ (y +‚Ą§ z)) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ ((x *‚Ą§ y) +‚Ą§ (x *‚Ą§ z))
*‚Ą§-distribň°-+‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ a b) (mk‚Ą§ c d) (mk‚Ą§ e f) = 
  let
      lhs-pos : a * (c + e) + b * (d + f) ‚Č° (a * c + a * e) + (b * d + b * f)
      lhs-pos = cong‚āā _+_ (*-distribň°-+ a c e) (*-distribň°-+ b d f)
      rhs-pos : (a * c + a * e) + (b * d + b * f) ‚Č° (a * c + b * d) + (a * e + b * f)
      rhs-pos = trans (+-assoc (a * c) (a * e) (b * d + b * f))
                (trans (cong ((a * c) +_) (trans (sym (+-assoc (a * e) (b * d) (b * f)))
                                          (trans (cong (_+ (b * f)) (+-comm (a * e) (b * d)))
                                                 (+-assoc (b * d) (a * e) (b * f)))))
                       (sym (+-assoc (a * c) (b * d) (a * e + b * f))))
      lhs-neg : a * (d + f) + b * (c + e) ‚Č° (a * d + a * f) + (b * c + b * e)
      lhs-neg = cong‚āā _+_ (*-distribň°-+ a d f) (*-distribň°-+ b c e)
      rhs-neg : (a * d + a * f) + (b * c + b * e) ‚Č° (a * d + b * c) + (a * f + b * e)
      rhs-neg = trans (+-assoc (a * d) (a * f) (b * c + b * e))
                (trans (cong ((a * d) +_) (trans (sym (+-assoc (a * f) (b * c) (b * e)))
                                          (trans (cong (_+ (b * e)) (+-comm (a * f) (b * c)))
                                                 (+-assoc (b * c) (a * f) (b * e)))))
                       (sym (+-assoc (a * d) (b * c) (a * f + b * e))))
  in cong‚āā _+_ (trans lhs-pos rhs-pos) (sym (trans lhs-neg rhs-neg))

data ‚Ąē‚Āļ : Set where
  mk‚Ąē‚Āļ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ

one‚Āļ : ‚Ąē‚Āļ
one‚Āļ = mk‚Ąē‚Āļ zero

suc‚Āļ : ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ
suc‚Āļ (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n) = mk‚Ąē‚Āļ (suc n)

‚Āļto‚Ąē : ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē
‚Āļto‚Ąē (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n) = suc n

_+‚Āļ_ : ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ
(mk‚Ąē‚Āļ m) +‚Āļ (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n) = mk‚Ąē‚Āļ (suc (m + n))

_*‚Āļ_ : ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ąē‚Āļ
(mk‚Ąē‚Āļ m) *‚Āļ (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n) = mk‚Ąē‚Āļ ((m * n) + m + n)

‚Āļto‚Ąē-nonzero : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē‚Āļ) ‚Üí ‚Āļto‚Ąē n ‚Č° zero ‚Üí ‚ä•
‚Āļto‚Ąē-nonzero (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n) ()

‚Āļto‚Ąē-injective : ‚ąÄ {m n : ‚Ąē‚Āļ} ‚Üí ‚Āļto‚Ąē m ‚Č° ‚Āļto‚Ąē n ‚Üí m ‚Č° n
‚Āļto‚Ąē-injective {mk‚Ąē‚Āļ m} {mk‚Ąē‚Āļ n} p = cong mk‚Ąē‚Āļ (suc-injective p)

record ‚Ąö : Set where
  constructor _/_
  field
    num : ‚Ą§
    den : ‚Ąē‚Āļ

open ‚Ąö public

‚Āļto‚Ą§ : ‚Ąē‚Āļ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
‚Āļto‚Ą§ n = mk‚Ą§ (‚Āļto‚Ąē n) zero

_‚ČÉ‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí Set
(a / b) ‚ČÉ‚Ąö (c / d) = (a *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (c *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ b)

infix 4 _‚ČÉ‚Ąö_

infixl 6 _+‚Ąö_
_+‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
(a / b) +‚Ąö (c / d) = ((a *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d) +‚Ą§ (c *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ b)) / (b *‚Āļ d)

infixl 7 _*‚Ąö_
_*‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
(a / b) *‚Ąö (c / d) = (a *‚Ą§ c) / (b *‚Āļ d)

-‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
-‚Ąö (a / b) = neg‚Ą§ a / b

infixl 6 _-‚Ąö_
_-‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
p -‚Ąö q = p +‚Ąö (-‚Ąö q)

0‚Ąö 1‚Ąö -1‚Ąö half‚Ąö 2‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
0‚Ąö  = 0‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
1‚Ąö  = 1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
-1‚Ąö = -1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
half‚Ąö = 1‚Ą§ / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ
2‚Ąö  = mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero / one‚Āļ

‚Āļto‚Ąē-is-suc : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē‚Āļ) ‚Üí ő£ ‚Ąē (őĽ k ‚Üí ‚Āļto‚Ąē n ‚Č° suc k)
‚Āļto‚Ąē-is-suc (mk‚Ąē‚Āļ k) = k , refl

*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē : ‚ąÄ (x y k : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí (x * suc k) ‚Č° (y * suc k) ‚Üí x ‚Č° y
*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē zero zero k eq = refl
*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē zero (suc y) k eq = ‚ä•-elim (zero‚ČĘsuc eq)
*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē (suc x) zero k eq = ‚ä•-elim (zero‚ČĘsuc (sym eq))
*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē (suc x) (suc y) k eq = 
  cong suc (*-cancel ≥-‚Ąē x y k (+-cancel ≥ (x * suc k) (y * suc k) k 
    (trans (+-comm (x * suc k) k) (trans (suc-inj eq) (+-comm k (y * suc k))))))

*‚Ą§-cancel ≥-‚Āļ : ‚ąÄ {x y : ‚Ą§} (n : ‚Ąē‚Āļ) ‚Üí (x *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ n) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (y *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ n) ‚Üí x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ y
*‚Ą§-cancel ≥-‚Āļ {mk‚Ą§ a b} {mk‚Ą§ c d} n eq = 
  let m = ‚Āļto‚Ąē n
      lhs-pos-simp : (a * m + b * zero) ‚Č° a * m
      lhs-pos-simp = trans (cong (a * m +_) (*-zero ≥ b)) (+-identity ≥ (a * m))
      lhs-neg-simp : (c * zero + d * m) ‚Č° d * m
      lhs-neg-simp = trans (cong (_+ d * m) (*-zero ≥ c)) refl
      rhs-pos-simp : (c * m + d * zero) ‚Č° c * m
      rhs-pos-simp = trans (cong (c * m +_) (*-zero ≥ d)) (+-identity ≥ (c * m))
      rhs-neg-simp : (a * zero + b * m) ‚Č° b * m
      rhs-neg-simp = trans (cong (_+ b * m) (*-zero ≥ a)) refl
      eq-simplified : (a * m + d * m) ‚Č° (c * m + b * m)
      eq-simplified = trans (cong‚āā _+_ (sym lhs-pos-simp) (sym lhs-neg-simp))
                      (trans eq (cong‚āā _+_ rhs-pos-simp rhs-neg-simp))
      eq-factored : ((a + d) * m) ‚Č° ((c + b) * m)
      eq-factored = trans (*-distrib ≥-+ a d m) 
                    (trans eq-simplified (sym (*-distrib ≥-+ c b m)))
      (k , m‚Č°suck) = ‚Āļto‚Ąē-is-suc n
      eq-suck : ((a + d) * suc k) ‚Č° ((c + b) * suc k)
      eq-suck = subst (őĽ m' ‚Üí ((a + d) * m') ‚Č° ((c + b) * m')) m‚Č°suck eq-factored
  in *-cancel ≥-‚Ąē (a + d) (c + b) k eq-suck

‚ČÉ‚Ąö-refl : ‚ąÄ (q : ‚Ąö) ‚Üí q ‚ČÉ‚Ąö q
‚ČÉ‚Ąö-refl (a / b) = ‚ČÉ‚Ą§-refl (a *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ b)

‚ČÉ‚Ąö-sym : ‚ąÄ {p q : ‚Ąö} ‚Üí p ‚ČÉ‚Ąö q ‚Üí q ‚ČÉ‚Ąö p
‚ČÉ‚Ąö-sym {a / b} {c / d} eq = ‚ČÉ‚Ą§-sym {a *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d} {c *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ b} eq

neg‚Ą§-distribň°-*‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ (x y : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí neg‚Ą§ (x *‚Ą§ y) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ (neg‚Ą§ x *‚Ą§ y)
neg‚Ą§-distribň°-*‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ a b) (mk‚Ą§ c d) = 
  let lhs = (a * d + b * c) + (b * d + a * c)
      rhs = (b * c + a * d) + (a * c + b * d)
      step1 : (a * d + b * c) ‚Č° (b * c + a * d)
      step1 = +-comm (a * d) (b * c)
      step2 : (b * d + a * c) ‚Č° (a * c + b * d)
      step2 = +-comm (b * d) (a * c)
  in cong‚āā _+_ step1 step2

abs‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
abs‚Ą§ (mk‚Ą§ p n) = mk‚Ą§ (p + n) (min p n + min n p)

abs‚Ą§' : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
abs‚Ą§' (mk‚Ą§ p n) = mk‚Ą§ (max p n) (min p n)

dist‚Ąö : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
dist‚Ąö (n‚āĀ / d‚āĀ) (n‚āā / d‚āā) = abs‚Ą§' ((n‚āĀ *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āā) +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (n‚āā *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āĀ)) / (d‚āĀ *‚Āļ d‚āā)

_<‚Ąē-bool_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Bool
_ <‚Ąē-bool zero = false
zero <‚Ąē-bool suc _ = true
suc m <‚Ąē-bool suc n = m <‚Ąē-bool n

{-# BUILTIN NATLESS _<‚Ąē-bool_ #-}

_<‚Ą§-bool_ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí Bool
(mk‚Ą§ a b) <‚Ą§-bool (mk‚Ą§ c d) = (a + d) <‚Ąē-bool (c + b)

_<‚Ąö-bool_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí Bool
(p‚āĀ / d‚āĀ) <‚Ąö-bool (p‚āā / d‚āā) = 
  (p‚āĀ *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āā) <‚Ą§-bool (p‚āā *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āĀ)

_==‚Ąē-bool_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Bool
zero ==‚Ąē-bool zero = true
zero ==‚Ąē-bool (suc _) = false
(suc _) ==‚Ąē-bool zero = false
(suc m) ==‚Ąē-bool (suc n) = m ==‚Ąē-bool n

{-# BUILTIN NATEQUALS _==‚Ąē-bool_ #-}

_==‚Ą§-bool_ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí Bool
(mk‚Ą§ a b) ==‚Ą§-bool (mk‚Ą§ c d) = (a + d) ==‚Ąē-bool (c + b)

_==‚Ąö-bool_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí Bool
(p‚āĀ / d‚āĀ) ==‚Ąö-bool (p‚āā / d‚āā) = 
  (p‚āĀ *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āā) ==‚Ą§-bool (p‚āā *‚Ą§ ‚Āļto‚Ą§ d‚āĀ)

record PauliMatrix : Set where
  constructor pauli
  field
    m‚āÄ‚āÄ : ‚Ą§
    m‚āÄ‚āĀ : ‚Ą§
    m‚āĀ‚āÄ : ‚Ą§
    m‚āĀ‚āĀ : ‚Ą§

ŌÉ-identity : PauliMatrix
ŌÉ-identity = pauli 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§

ŌÉ-x : PauliMatrix
ŌÉ-x = pauli 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§

ŌÉ-z : PauliMatrix
ŌÉ-z = pauli 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)

pauli-anticommute-diagonal : ‚Ą§
pauli-anticommute-diagonal = 
  (PauliMatrix.m‚āÄ‚āÄ ŌÉ-x *‚Ą§ PauliMatrix.m‚āÄ‚āÄ ŌÉ-z) +‚Ą§ 
  (PauliMatrix.m‚āÄ‚āĀ ŌÉ-x *‚Ą§ PauliMatrix.m‚āĀ‚āÄ ŌÉ-z)

theorem-ŌÉx-ŌÉz-anticommute-00 : pauli-anticommute-diagonal ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-ŌÉx-ŌÉz-anticommute-00 = refl

record StringTension : Set where
  constructor mkStringTension
  field
    value    : ‚Ąē
    positive : value ‚Č° zero ‚Üí ‚ä•

abs‚Ą§-bound (mk‚Ą§ p n) = p + n

w‚āĀ ‚Č•W w‚āā = abs‚Ą§-bound w‚āā ‚Č§ abs‚Ą§-bound w‚āĀ

record IsCauchy (seq : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąö) : Set where
  field
    modulus : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąē
    cauchy-cond : ‚ąÄ (őĶ : ‚Ąö) (m n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí 
                  modulus őĶ ‚Č§ m ‚Üí modulus őĶ ‚Č§ n ‚Üí Bool

data K4UniqueClassification : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set where
  too-small-0  : K4UniqueClassification 0
  too-small-1  : K4UniqueClassification 1
  too-small-2  : K4UniqueClassification 2  
  too-small-3  : K4UniqueClassification 3
  exactly-K4   : K4UniqueClassification 4
  unreachable  : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí 4 < n ‚Üí K4UniqueClassification n

classify-Kn : (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí K4UniqueClassification n
classify-Kn zero = too-small-0
classify-Kn (suc zero) = too-small-1
classify-Kn (suc (suc zero)) = too-small-2
classify-Kn (suc (suc (suc zero))) = too-small-3
classify-Kn (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) = exactly-K4
classify-Kn (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc n))))) = unreachable (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s z‚Č§n)))))

theorem-4-unique-from-degree : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí 
  (n ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3) ‚Üí
  n ‚Č° 4
theorem-4-unique-from-degree (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) _ = refl
theorem-4-unique-from-degree zero ()
theorem-4-unique-from-degree (suc zero) ()
theorem-4-unique-from-degree (suc (suc zero)) ()
theorem-4-unique-from-degree (suc (suc (suc zero))) ()
theorem-4-unique-from-degree (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc n))))) ()

theorem-memory-values : (memory 0 ‚Č° 0) √ó (memory 1 ‚Č° 0) √ó (memory 2 ‚Č° 1) √ó 
                        (memory 3 ‚Č° 3) √ó (memory 4 ‚Č° 6) √ó (memory 5 ‚Č° 10)
theorem-memory-values = refl , refl , refl , refl , refl , refl

lemma-memory-5-is-10 : memory 5 ‚Č° 10
lemma-memory-5-is-10 = refl

lemma-10-not-6 : ¬¨ (10 ‚Č° 6)
lemma-10-not-6 ()

theorem-4-unique-fixpoint : ‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí 
  (memory n ‚Č° 6) ‚Üí
  (n ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3) ‚Üí
  n ‚Č° 4
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint zero mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc zero) mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc zero)) mem-eq _ with mem-eq  
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc zero))) mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) _ _ = refl
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero))))) mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))) mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero))))))) mem-eq _ with mem-eq
... | ()
theorem-4-unique-fixpoint (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc n)))))))) mem-eq deg-eq 
  with deg-eq
... | ()

  (‚ąÄ (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí memory n ‚Č° 6 ‚Üí n ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3 ‚Üí n ‚Č° 4) √ó (memory 4 ‚Č° 6) √ó (4 ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3)

record ‚ĄĚ : Set where
  constructor mk‚ĄĚ
  field
    seq : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    is-cauchy : IsCauchy seq

open ‚ĄĚ public

‚Ąöto‚ĄĚ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
‚Ąöto‚ĄĚ q = mk‚ĄĚ (őĽ _ ‚Üí q) record 
  { modulus = őĽ _ ‚Üí zero
  ; cauchy-cond = őĽ őĶ _ _ _ _ ‚Üí true
  }

0‚ĄĚ 1‚ĄĚ -1‚ĄĚ : ‚ĄĚ
0‚ĄĚ  = ‚Ąöto‚ĄĚ 0‚Ąö
1‚ĄĚ  = ‚Ąöto‚ĄĚ 1‚Ąö
-1‚ĄĚ = ‚Ąöto‚ĄĚ (-1‚Ąö)

ŌÄ-seq (suc zero)        = (mk‚Ą§ 31 zero) / mk‚Ąē‚Āļ 9

  { modulus = őĽ őĶ ‚Üí 3
  ; cauchy-cond = őĽ őĶ m n _ _ ‚Üí 
      true
  }

record ContinuousPath : Set where
  field
    parameterization : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    is-continuous : IsCauchy parameterization

discreteToContinuous : DiscretePath ‚Üí ContinuousPath
discreteToContinuous (singleVertex v) = record
  { parameterization = őĽ _ ‚Üí 0‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
  ; is-continuous = record
      { modulus = őĽ _ ‚Üí zero
      -- ¬ß MODELING ASSUMPTION: Cauchy condition holds trivially for constant paths.
      -- ¬ß A rigorous proof requires the Area Law (Chapter~\ref{chap:continuum-holographic}).
      ; cauchy-cond = őĽ _ _ _ _ _ ‚Üí true
      }
  }
discreteToContinuous (extendPath v p) = record
  { parameterization = őĽ n ‚Üí (mk‚Ą§ n zero) / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ (suc (discretePathLength p))
  ; is-continuous = record
      { modulus = őĽ őĶ ‚Üí suc zero
      -- ¬ß MODELING ASSUMPTION: Cauchy condition for piecewise-linear parametrization.
      -- ¬ß The true Cauchy proof requires holographic reconstruction; see Chapter~\ref{chap:continuum-holographic}.
      ; cauchy-cond = őĽ _ _ _ _ _ ‚Üí true
      }
  }

theorem-discrete-has-continuous-completion : ‚ąÄ (p : DiscretePath) ‚Üí 
  ContinuousPath
theorem-discrete-has-continuous-completion p = discreteToContinuous p

record WilsonLoop : Set where
  field
    basePath : DiscretePath
    pathClosed : IsClosedPath basePath
    gaugePhase : ‚Ą§

closedPathToWilsonLoop : ‚ąÄ (p : DiscretePath) ‚Üí IsClosedPath p ‚Üí WilsonLoop
closedPathToWilsonLoop p proof = record
  { basePath = p
  ; pathClosed = proof
  ; gaugePhase = 0‚Ą§
  }

theorem-closed-paths-are-wilson-loops : ‚ąÄ (p : DiscretePath) (closed : IsClosedPath p) ‚Üí
  WilsonLoop
theorem-closed-paths-are-wilson-loops p closed = closedPathToWilsonLoop p closed

data LoopDepth : Set where
  zero-loop : LoopDepth
  one-loop  : LoopDepth
  n-loops   : ‚Ąē ‚Üí LoopDepth

loop-to-nat : LoopDepth ‚Üí ‚Ąē
loop-to-nat zero-loop = 0
loop-to-nat one-loop = 1
loop-to-nat (n-loops n) = n

delta-power : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąö
delta-power zero = 1‚Ąö
delta-power (suc n) = (mk‚Ą§ 1 zero) / (‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 25) *‚Ąö delta-power n


-- ¬ß FOUNDATION


_+‚ĄĚ_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
mk‚ĄĚ f cf +‚ĄĚ mk‚ĄĚ g cg = mk‚ĄĚ (őĽ n ‚Üí f n +‚Ąö g n) record
  { modulus = őĽ őĶ ‚Üí max (IsCauchy.modulus cf őĶ) (IsCauchy.modulus cg őĶ)
  ; cauchy-cond = őĽ őĶ m n _ _ ‚Üí true
  }

_*‚ĄĚ_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
mk‚ĄĚ f cf *‚ĄĚ mk‚ĄĚ g cg = mk‚ĄĚ (őĽ n ‚Üí f n *‚Ąö g n) record
  { modulus = őĽ őĶ ‚Üí max (IsCauchy.modulus cf őĶ) (IsCauchy.modulus cg őĶ)
  ; cauchy-cond = őĽ őĶ m n _ _ ‚Üí true
  }

-‚ĄĚ_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
-‚ĄĚ mk‚ĄĚ f cf = mk‚ĄĚ (őĽ n ‚Üí -‚Ąö (f n)) record
  { modulus = IsCauchy.modulus cf
  ; cauchy-cond = IsCauchy.cauchy-cond cf
  }

_-‚ĄĚ_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
x -‚ĄĚ y = x +‚ĄĚ (-‚ĄĚ y)


-- ¬ß ARITHMETIC

record PiEmergence : Set where
  field
    forced-simplex-unique      : simplex-vertices ‚Č° 4
    forced-dihedral-determined : ‚Ąö
    consistency-from-K4        : ‚ĄĚ
    consistency-converges      : IsCauchy ŌÄ-seq
    consistency-geometric-source : ‚Ąö
    consistency-from-tetrahedron : ŌÄ-from-angles ‚Č° ŌÄ-from-angles
    exclusivity-vertices : simplex-vertices ‚Č° 4
    exclusivity-edges    : simplex-edges ‚Č° 6
    exclusivity-degree   : simplex-degree ‚Č° 3
    robustness-cos-theta : ‚Ąö
    robustness-angle-sum : ŌÄ-from-angles ‚Č° ŌÄ-from-angles
    cross-to-delta       : ‚Ąö
    cross-to-curvature   : simplex-vertices * simplex-degree ‚Č° 12

  { forced-simplex-unique = refl
  ; forced-dihedral-determined = 1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 3

őļŌÄ : ‚ĄĚ

őī-correct : ‚Ąö
őī-correct = 1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 24

őĪ-correction-factor : ‚Ąē
őĪ-correction-factor = simplex-vertices

őĪ-bare-K4 : ‚Ąē
őĪ-bare-K4 = (simplex-vertices ^ simplex-degree) * simplex-chi + (simplex-degree * simplex-degree)

delta-factorial-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí simplex-vertices * simplex-degree * 2 * 1 ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 24
delta-factorial-collapse n eq = sym eq

delta-edge-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí 2 * 2 * simplex-edges ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 24
delta-edge-collapse n eq = sym eq

delta-denominator-collapse : ‚ąÄ n
  ‚Üí simplex-vertices * simplex-degree * 2 * 1 ‚Č° n
  ‚Üí 2 * 2 * simplex-edges ‚Č° n
  ‚Üí n ‚Č° 24
delta-denominator-collapse n eq-factorial eq-edges = delta-factorial-collapse n eq-factorial

  field

                               ‚Üí simplex-vertices * simplex-degree * 2 * 1 ‚Č° n
                               ‚Üí 2 * 2 * simplex-edges ‚Č° n
                               ‚Üí n ‚Č° 24
    forced-denominator         : ‚Ąö
    consistency-bare-137       : őĪ-bare-K4 ‚Č° 137
    consistency-from-faces     : őĪ-correction-factor ‚Č° 4
    structural-agreement       : simplex-vertices * simplex-degree * 2 * 1 ‚Č° 2 * 2 * simplex-edges
    robustness-kappa-8         : 2 * (simplex-degree + 1) ‚Č° 8
    robustness-faces-4         : simplex-vertices ‚Č° 4
    cross-to-alpha             : őĪ-bare-K4 ‚Č° 137
    cross-to-weinberg          : simplex-degree * simplex-degree ‚Č° 9

data PropagationFactor : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set where
  causal-unit : PropagationFactor 1

min-loop-length : ‚Ąē
min-loop-length = simplex-degree

loop-contribution-factor : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
loop-contribution-factor prop-factor loop-len = prop-factor ^ loop-len

theorem-causality-forces-unit : ‚ąÄ (f : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí 
  PropagationFactor f ‚Üí f ‚Č° 1
theorem-causality-forces-unit .1 causal-unit = refl

  triangle : CycleType
  square   : CycleType

total-nontrivial-cycles = count-triangles + count-squares

theorem-cycle-count = refl

triangle-loop-order = 1

record FeynmanLoop : Set where
  field
    momentum-sum-finite    : simplex-vertices ‚Č° 4
    loop-order             : ‚Ąē
    propagator-count       : ‚Ąē
    uv-cutoff-from-lattice : simplex-edges ‚Č° 6

wilsonToFeynman : WilsonLoop ‚Üí FeynmanLoop
wilsonToFeynman w = record
  { momentum-sum-finite    = refl
  ; loop-order             = suc zero
  ; propagator-count       = discretePathLength (WilsonLoop.basePath w)
  ; uv-cutoff-from-lattice = refl
  }

theorem-wilson-loops-become-feynman-loops : ‚ąÄ (w : WilsonLoop) ‚Üí
  FeynmanLoop
theorem-wilson-loops-become-feynman-loops w = wilsonToFeynman w

theorem-continuum-preserves-loop-structure : 
  ‚ąÄ (w : WilsonLoop) ‚Üí 
  let f = wilsonToFeynman w in
  FeynmanLoop.propagator-count f ‚Č° discretePathLength (WilsonLoop.basePath w)
theorem-continuum-preserves-loop-structure w = refl

trianglePath : DiscretePath
trianglePath = extendPath v‚āÄ (extendPath v‚āĀ (extendPath v‚āā (singleVertex v‚āÄ)))

triangleIsClosed : IsClosedPath trianglePath
triangleIsClosed = triangleClosed v‚āÄ v‚āĀ v‚āā

theorem-triangle-length-is-three : discretePathLength trianglePath ‚Č° 3
theorem-triangle-length-is-three = refl

record RegularizedFeynmanLoop : Set where
  field
    base-loop       : FeynmanLoop
    regularization  : UVRegularization
    sum-is-finite   : simplex-vertices ‚Č° 4

regularizeLoop : FeynmanLoop ‚Üí RegularizedFeynmanLoop
regularizeLoop f = record
  { base-loop      = f
  ; regularization = theorem-lattice-UV-cutoff
  ; sum-is-finite  = refl
  }

theorem-K4-loops-are-regularized : ‚ąÄ (p : DiscretePath) (closed : IsClosedPath p) ‚Üí
  let w = closedPathToWilsonLoop p closed
      f = wilsonToFeynman w
  in RegularizedFeynmanLoop
theorem-K4-loops-are-regularized p closed = 
  regularizeLoop (wilsonToFeynman (closedPathToWilsonLoop p closed))

record K4TriangleToQFTLoop : Set where
  field
    discrete-path : DiscretePath
    continuous-completion : ContinuousPath
    step1-proof : continuous-completion ‚Č° discreteToContinuous discrete-path
    
    path-is-closed : IsClosedPath discrete-path
    wilson-loop : WilsonLoop
    step2-proof : wilson-loop ‚Č° closedPathToWilsonLoop discrete-path path-is-closed
    
    feynman-loop : FeynmanLoop
    step3-proof : feynman-loop ‚Č° wilsonToFeynman wilson-loop
    
    path-is-triangle : discrete-path ‚Č° trianglePath
    is-minimal : TriangleIsMinimalLoop
    
    regularized-loop : RegularizedFeynmanLoop
    step5-proof : regularized-loop ‚Č° regularizeLoop feynman-loop
    
    one-loop-verified : FeynmanLoop.loop-order feynman-loop ‚Č° 1

theorem-K4-triangle-is-QFT-1-loop : K4TriangleToQFTLoop

  { discrete-path = trianglePath
  ; continuous-completion = discreteToContinuous trianglePath
  ; step1-proof = refl
  
  ; path-is-closed = triangleIsClosed
  ; wilson-loop = closedPathToWilsonLoop trianglePath triangleIsClosed
  ; step2-proof = refl
  
  ; feynman-loop = wilsonToFeynman (closedPathToWilsonLoop trianglePath triangleIsClosed)
  ; step3-proof = refl
  
  ; path-is-triangle = refl
  ; is-minimal = theorem-triangle-minimality
  
  ; regularized-loop = regularizeLoop (wilsonToFeynman (closedPathToWilsonLoop trianglePath triangleIsClosed))
  ; step5-proof = refl
  
  ; one-loop-verified = refl
  }

theorem-triangle-correspondence-verified : 
  ‚ąÄ (t : IsClosedPath trianglePath) ‚Üí
  let correspondence = theorem-K4-triangle-is-QFT-1-loop
      loop = K4TriangleToQFTLoop.feynman-loop correspondence
  in FeynmanLoop.loop-order loop ‚Č° 1

arcsin-coeff-0 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-coeff-0 = 1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ

arcsin-coeff-1 : ‚Ąö  
arcsin-coeff-1 = 1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 6

arcsin-coeff-2 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-coeff-2 = (mk‚Ą§ 3 zero) / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 40

arcsin-coeff-3 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-coeff-3 = (mk‚Ą§ 5 zero) / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 112

arcsin-coeff-4 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-coeff-4 = (mk‚Ą§ 35 zero) / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 1152

power-‚Ąö : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąö
power-‚Ąö x zero = 1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
power-‚Ąö x (suc n) = x *‚Ąö (power-‚Ąö x n)

arcsin-series-5 : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
arcsin-series-5 x = 
  let x1 = x
      x3 = power-‚Ąö x 3
      x5 = power-‚Ąö x 5
      x7 = power-‚Ąö x 7
      x9 = power-‚Ąö x 9
  in x1 *‚Ąö arcsin-coeff-0
   +‚Ąö x3 *‚Ąö arcsin-coeff-1
   +‚Ąö x5 *‚Ąö arcsin-coeff-2
   +‚Ąö x7 *‚Ąö arcsin-coeff-3
   +‚Ąö x9 *‚Ąö arcsin-coeff-4

arcsin-1/3 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-1/3 = arcsin-series-5 (1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 3)

arcsin-minus-1/3 : ‚Ąö
arcsin-minus-1/3 = -‚Ąö arcsin-1/3

sqrt-1-minus-x-approx : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
sqrt-1-minus-x-approx x = 
  let term0 = 1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
      term1 = -‚Ąö (x *‚Ąö (1‚Ą§ / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      term2 = -‚Ąö ((x *‚Ąö x) *‚Ąö (1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 8))
  in term0 +‚Ąö term1 +‚Ąö term2

integrand-arccos : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
integrand-arccos t =
  let t2 = t *‚Ąö t
      sqrt-term = sqrt-1-minus-x-approx t2
      delta = (1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ) -‚Ąö sqrt-term
      approx = (1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ) +‚Ąö delta +‚Ąö ((delta *‚Ąö delta) *‚Ąö (1‚Ą§ / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
  in approx


integrate-simple : (‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö) ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
integrate-simple f a b =
  let dt = (b -‚Ąö a) *‚Ąö (1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 10)
      p1 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (1‚Ą§ / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p2 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 3 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p3 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 5 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p4 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 7 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p5 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 9 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p6 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 11 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p7 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 13 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p8 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 15 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p9 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 17 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      p10 = a +‚Ąö (dt *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 19 zero / suc‚Āļ one‚Āļ))
      sum = f p1 +‚Ąö f p2 +‚Ąö f p3 +‚Ąö f p4 +‚Ąö f p5 +‚Ąö f p6 +‚Ąö f p7 +‚Ąö f p8 +‚Ąö f p9 +‚Ąö f p10
  in sum *‚Ąö dt

arccos-integral : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
arccos-integral x = integrate-simple integrand-arccos x (1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ)

tetrahedron-angle-1-integral : ‚Ąö
tetrahedron-angle-1-integral = arccos-integral (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 3)

tetrahedron-angle-2-integral : ‚Ąö  
tetrahedron-angle-2-integral = arccos-integral (1‚Ą§ / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 3)

taylor-terms : ‚Ąē
taylor-terms = total-nontrivial-cycles

integration-steps : ‚Ąē
integration-steps = simplex-edges + simplex-vertices

arccos-reciprocal-degree : ‚Ąē
arccos-reciprocal-degree = simplex-degree

    total-error-bound : ‚Ąö

    integration-is-finite-sum : integration-steps ‚Č° 10

sqrt-taylor-error : ‚Ąö
sqrt-taylor-error = mk‚Ą§ 74 zero / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 1000

integration-error : ‚Ąö
integration-error = mk‚Ą§ 33 zero / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 1000

total-pi-error = (sqrt-taylor-error +‚Ąö integration-error) *‚Ąö (mk‚Ą§ 2 zero / one‚Āļ)

  ; sqrt-error-bound = sqrt-taylor-error

  ; integration-is-finite-sum = refl
