-- ¬ß DRIFT

data MassContribution : Set where
  degree-power : ‚Ąē ‚Üí MassContribution
  euler-power  : ‚Ąē ‚Üí MassContribution
  fermat-prime : ‚Ąē ‚Üí MassContribution
  boundary-sum : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí MassContribution

contribution-signature : MassContribution ‚Üí ArithmeticSignature
contribution-signature (degree-power _) = divergent
contribution-signature (euler-power _)  = divergent
contribution-signature (fermat-prime _) = divergent
contribution-signature (boundary-sum _ _) = convergent

contribution-value : MassContribution ‚Üí ‚Ąē
contribution-value (degree-power n) = degree-K4 ^ n
contribution-value (euler-power n)  = eulerChar-computed ^ n
contribution-value (fermat-prime 0) = 3
contribution-value (fermat-prime 1) = 5
contribution-value (fermat-prime 2) = F‚āā
contribution-value (fermat-prime (suc (suc (suc _)))) = F‚āÉ
contribution-value (boundary-sum a b) = a + b

muon-contributions : MassContribution √ó MassContribution
muon-contributions = degree-power 2 , boundary-sum edgeCountK4 F‚āā

proton-contribution-chi : MassContribution
proton-contribution-chi = euler-power 2

proton-contribution-vol : MassContribution
proton-contribution-vol = degree-power 3

proton-contribution-ground : MassContribution
proton-contribution-ground = fermat-prime 2

theorem-muon-from-meta-rule : 
  let (surf , bnd) = muon-contributions
  in contribution-value surf * contribution-value bnd ‚Č° 207
theorem-muon-from-meta-rule = refl

theorem-proton-from-meta-rule :
  contribution-value proton-contribution-chi * 
  contribution-value proton-contribution-vol * 
  contribution-value proton-contribution-ground ‚Č° 1836
theorem-proton-from-meta-rule = refl


-- ¬ß PLUSONE

record PlusOne-5Pillar : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    compactified-vertices-forced : suc vertexCountK4 ‚Č° 5
    compactified-spinors-forced : suc clifford-dimension ‚Č° 17
    compactified-couplings-forced : suc EdgePairCount-early ‚Č° 37
    spinor-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí suc clifford-dimension ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 17
    vertex-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí suc vertexCountK4 ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 5
    coupling-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí suc EdgePairCount-early ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 37
    universal-property : (A : Set) ‚Üí PlusOne-Forced-By-Universality A
    admissible-collapse : (A : Set) ‚Üí (E : AdmissiblePointExtension A) ‚Üí FreePointedCollapse A E
    plus-zero-eliminated : ¬¨ (suc clifford-dimension ‚Č° 16)
    plus-two-eliminated : ¬¨ (suc clifford-dimension ‚Č° 18)
    basepoint-distinct : (s : Fin 16) ‚Üí ¬¨ (embed s ‚Č° ‚ąě)
    external-point-unique : ‚ąÄ (d‚āĀ d‚āĀ' : D‚āĀ) ‚Üí observer-D‚āĀ-to-‚ąě d‚āĀ ‚Č° observer-D‚āĀ-to-‚ąě d‚āĀ'
    vertices-stable : vertexCountK4 ‚Č° 4
    spinors-stable : clifford-dimension ‚Č° 16
    couplings-stable : EdgePairCount-early ‚Č° 36
    observer-exists : D‚āĀ
    observer-contains-observed : D‚āĀ ‚Üí D‚āÄ
    centroid-matches : fst centroid-barycentric ‚Č° 1
    convergence : vertexCountK4 + faceCountK4 ‚Č° edgeCountK4 + eulerChar-computed

theorem-plus-one-5pillar : PlusOne-5Pillar
theorem-plus-one-5pillar = record
  { compactified-vertices-forced = refl
  ; compactified-spinors-forced = theorem-F‚āā-is-17
  ; compactified-couplings-forced = theorem-37-is-compactification
  ; spinor-collapse = compactified-spinor-count-collapse
  ; vertex-collapse = compactified-vertex-count-collapse
  ; coupling-collapse = compactified-coupling-count-collapse
  ; universal-property = theorem-plus-one-universal
  ; admissible-collapse = őĽ A E ‚Üí theorem-admissible-extension-collapses E
  ; plus-zero-eliminated = plus-zero-eliminated-spinor
  ; plus-two-eliminated = plus-two-eliminated-spinor
  ; basepoint-distinct = embed-not-infinity
  ; external-point-unique = theorem-single-infinity
  ; vertices-stable = refl
  ; spinors-stable = refl
  ; couplings-stable = refl
  ; observer-exists = canonical-D‚āĀ
  ; observer-contains-observed = D‚āĀ-to-D‚āÄ
  ; centroid-matches = refl
  ; convergence = refl
  }

ObserverForcesPlus1 : Set‚āĀ
ObserverForcesPlus1 = PlusOne-5Pillar

theorem-observer-forces-plus-1 : ObserverForcesPlus1
theorem-observer-forces-plus-1 = theorem-plus-one-5pillar


-- ¬ß K4-GRAPH

module EndoModule (d : AbstractDistinction) where

  interpret : EndoCase ‚Üí (S d ‚Üí S d)
  interpret case-constL _ = ad-‚Ąď d
  interpret case-constR _ = ad-r d
  interpret case-id     x = x
  interpret case-dual     = AD-dual d

  classify : (S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí EndoCase
  classify f with ad-cover d (f (ad-‚Ąď d)) | ad-cover d (f (ad-r d))
  ... | inj‚āĀ _ | inj‚āĀ _ = case-constL
  ... | inj‚āā _ | inj‚āā _ = case-constR
  ... | inj‚āĀ _ | inj‚āā _ = case-id
  ... | inj‚āā _ | inj‚āĀ _ = case-dual

  sound-at-‚Ąď : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
               interpret (classify f) (ad-‚Ąď d) ‚Č° f (ad-‚Ąď d)
  sound-at-‚Ąď f with ad-cover d (f (ad-‚Ąď d)) | ad-cover d (f (ad-r d))
  ... | inj‚āĀ fl‚Č°‚Ąď | inj‚āĀ _     = sym fl‚Č°‚Ąď
  ... | inj‚āā fl‚Č°r | inj‚āā _     = sym fl‚Č°r
  ... | inj‚āĀ fl‚Č°‚Ąď | inj‚āā _     = sym fl‚Č°‚Ąď
  ... | inj‚āā fl‚Č°r | inj‚āĀ _     = trans (AD-dual-‚Ąď d) (sym fl‚Č°r)

  sound-at-r : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
               interpret (classify f) (ad-r d) ‚Č° f (ad-r d)
  sound-at-r f with ad-cover d (f (ad-‚Ąď d)) | ad-cover d (f (ad-r d))
  ... | inj‚āĀ _     | inj‚āĀ fr‚Č°‚Ąď = sym fr‚Č°‚Ąď
  ... | inj‚āā _     | inj‚āā fr‚Č°r = sym fr‚Č°r
  ... | inj‚āĀ _     | inj‚āā fr‚Č°r = sym fr‚Č°r
  ... | inj‚āā _     | inj‚āĀ fr‚Č°‚Ąď = trans (AD-dual-r d) (sym fr‚Č°‚Ąď)

  classify-sound : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                   (x : S d) ‚Üí interpret (classify f) x ‚Č° f x
  classify-sound f = AD-determined d
    (interpret (classify f)) f
    (sound-at-‚Ąď f) (sound-at-r f)

  absurd-‚Ąďr : {A : Set} ‚Üí ad-‚Ąď d ‚Č° ad-r d ‚Üí A
  absurd-‚Ąďr e = ‚ä•-elim (ad-‚Ąď‚Č†r d e)

  interpret-injective :
    (c c' : EndoCase) ‚Üí
    ((x : S d) ‚Üí interpret c x ‚Č° interpret c' x) ‚Üí
    c ‚Č° c'
  interpret-injective case-constL case-constL _ = refl
  interpret-injective case-constL case-constR p = absurd-‚Ąďr (p (ad-‚Ąď d))
  interpret-injective case-constL case-id     p = absurd-‚Ąďr (p (ad-r d))
  interpret-injective case-constL case-dual   p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (trans (p (ad-‚Ąď d)) (AD-dual-‚Ąď d))
  interpret-injective case-constR case-constL p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (p (ad-‚Ąď d)))
  interpret-injective case-constR case-constR _ = refl
  interpret-injective case-constR case-id     p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (p (ad-‚Ąď d)))
  interpret-injective case-constR case-dual   p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (trans (p (ad-r d)) (AD-dual-r d)))
  interpret-injective case-id case-constL     p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (p (ad-r d)))
  interpret-injective case-id case-constR     p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (p (ad-‚Ąď d))
  interpret-injective case-id case-id         _ = refl
  interpret-injective case-id case-dual       p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (trans (p (ad-‚Ąď d)) (AD-dual-‚Ąď d))
  interpret-injective case-dual case-constL   p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (trans (sym (AD-dual-‚Ąď d)) (p (ad-‚Ąď d))))
  interpret-injective case-dual case-constR   p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (trans (sym (AD-dual-r d)) (p (ad-r d)))
  interpret-injective case-dual case-id       p =
    absurd-‚Ąďr (sym (trans (sym (AD-dual-‚Ąď d)) (p (ad-‚Ąď d))))
  interpret-injective case-dual case-dual     _ = refl

  -- ¬ß Every endomorphism has a witness in EndoCase (existence + soundness)
  endo-witness : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                 ő£ EndoCase (őĽ c ‚Üí (x : S d) ‚Üí interpret c x ‚Č° f x)
  endo-witness f = classify f , classify-sound f

  -- ¬ß The witness is unique
  endo-unique : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                (c‚āĀ c‚āā : EndoCase) ‚Üí
                ((x : S d) ‚Üí interpret c‚āĀ x ‚Č° f x) ‚Üí
                ((x : S d) ‚Üí interpret c‚āā x ‚Č° f x) ‚Üí
                c‚āĀ ‚Č° c‚āā
  endo-unique f c‚āĀ c‚āā p‚āĀ p‚āā =
    interpret-injective c‚āĀ c‚āā
      (őĽ x ‚Üí trans (p‚āĀ x) (sym (p‚āā x)))

-- ¬ß Re-export module contents for use in subsequent chapters.
AD-interpret : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí EndoCase ‚Üí (S d ‚Üí S d)
AD-interpret d = EndoModule.interpret d

AD-classify : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí (S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí EndoCase
AD-classify d = EndoModule.classify d

AD-classify-sound : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                    (x : S d) ‚Üí EndoModule.interpret d (EndoModule.classify d f) x ‚Č° f x
AD-classify-sound d = EndoModule.classify-sound d

AD-absurd-‚Ąďr : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí {A : Set} ‚Üí ad-‚Ąď d ‚Č° ad-r d ‚Üí A
AD-absurd-‚Ąďr d = EndoModule.absurd-‚Ąďr d

AD-interpret-injective : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí
  (c c' : EndoCase) ‚Üí
  ((x : S d) ‚Üí EndoModule.interpret d c x ‚Č° EndoModule.interpret d c' x) ‚Üí
  c ‚Č° c'
AD-interpret-injective d = EndoModule.interpret-injective d

AD-endo-witness : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                  ő£ EndoCase (őĽ c ‚Üí (x : S d) ‚Üí EndoModule.interpret d c x ‚Č° f x)
AD-endo-witness d = EndoModule.endo-witness d

AD-endo-unique : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí
                 (c‚āĀ c‚āā : EndoCase) ‚Üí
                 ((x : S d) ‚Üí EndoModule.interpret d c‚āĀ x ‚Č° f x) ‚Üí
                 ((x : S d) ‚Üí EndoModule.interpret d c‚āā x ‚Č° f x) ‚Üí
                 c‚āĀ ‚Č° c‚āā
AD-endo-unique d = EndoModule.endo-unique d

-- ¬ß Decidable equality on EndoCase
EndoCase-eq? : (c‚āĀ c‚āā : EndoCase) ‚Üí (c‚āĀ ‚Č° c‚āā) ‚äé (c‚āĀ ‚ČĘ c‚āā)
EndoCase-eq? case-constL case-constL = inj‚āĀ refl
EndoCase-eq? case-constL case-constR = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-constL case-id     = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-constL case-dual   = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-constR case-constL = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-constR case-constR = inj‚āĀ refl
EndoCase-eq? case-constR case-id     = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-constR case-dual   = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-id     case-constL = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-id     case-constR = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-id     case-id     = inj‚āĀ refl
EndoCase-eq? case-id     case-dual   = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-dual   case-constL = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-dual   case-constR = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-dual   case-id     = inj‚āā (őĽ ())
EndoCase-eq? case-dual   case-dual   = inj‚āĀ refl

EndoCase-to-Fin4 : EndoCase ‚Üí Fin 4
EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-constL = zero
EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-constR = suc zero
EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-id     = suc (suc zero)
EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-dual   = suc (suc (suc zero))

Fin4-to-EndoCase : Fin 4 ‚Üí EndoCase
Fin4-to-EndoCase zero                      = case-constL
Fin4-to-EndoCase (suc zero)                = case-constR
Fin4-to-EndoCase (suc (suc zero))          = case-id
Fin4-to-EndoCase (suc (suc (suc zero)))    = case-dual

EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ : (c : EndoCase) ‚Üí Fin4-to-EndoCase (EndoCase-to-Fin4 c) ‚Č° c
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ case-constL = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ case-constR = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ case-id     = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ case-dual   = refl

EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āā : (f : Fin 4) ‚Üí EndoCase-to-Fin4 (Fin4-to-EndoCase f) ‚Č° f
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āā zero                      = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āā (suc zero)                = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āā (suc (suc zero))          = refl
EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āā (suc (suc (suc zero)))    = refl

-- ¬ß K‚āĄ edge: any two distinct endomorphism cases
record EndoPresentation (d : AbstractDistinction) (X : Set) : Set where
  field
    ep-interpret : X ‚Üí (S d ‚Üí S d)
    ep-classify  : (S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí X
    ep-sound     : (f : S d ‚Üí S d) ‚Üí (x : S d) ‚Üí
                   ep-interpret (ep-classify f) x ‚Č° f x
    ep-injective : (a b : X) ‚Üí
                   ((x : S d) ‚Üí ep-interpret a x ‚Č° ep-interpret b x) ‚Üí
                   a ‚Č° b

-- ¬ß EndoCase is itself a valid presentation
EndoCase-presentation : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí EndoPresentation d EndoCase
EndoCase-presentation d = record
  { ep-interpret = AD-interpret d
  ; ep-classify  = AD-classify d
  ; ep-sound     = AD-classify-sound d
  ; ep-injective = AD-interpret-injective d
  }

-- ¬ß Any other presentation is isomorphic to EndoCase
theorem-presentation-unique : (d : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí
  {X : Set} ‚Üí EndoPresentation d X ‚Üí
  ő£ (X ‚Üí EndoCase) (őĽ to ‚Üí
  ő£ (EndoCase ‚Üí X) (őĽ from ‚Üí
  ((c : EndoCase) ‚Üí to (from c) ‚Č° c) √ó
  ((x : X) ‚Üí from (to x) ‚Č° x)))
theorem-presentation-unique d {X} pres =
  to' , from' , to-from' , from-to'
  where
    to' : X ‚Üí EndoCase
    to' x = AD-classify d (EndoPresentation.ep-interpret pres x)

    from' : EndoCase ‚Üí X
    from' c = EndoPresentation.ep-classify pres (AD-interpret d c)

    to-from' : (c : EndoCase) ‚Üí to' (from' c) ‚Č° c
    to-from' c = AD-endo-unique d
      (EndoPresentation.ep-interpret pres (from' c))
      (AD-classify d (EndoPresentation.ep-interpret pres (from' c)))
      c
      (AD-classify-sound d (EndoPresentation.ep-interpret pres (from' c)))
      (őĽ x ‚Üí sym (EndoPresentation.ep-sound pres (AD-interpret d c) x))

    from-to' : (x : X) ‚Üí from' (to' x) ‚Č° x
    from-to' x = EndoPresentation.ep-injective pres
      (from' (to' x)) x
      (őĽ v ‚Üí trans
        (EndoPresentation.ep-sound pres (AD-interpret d (to' x)) v)
        (AD-classify-sound d (EndoPresentation.ep-interpret pres x) v))

-- ¬ß Classification of maps between two (possibly different) abstract distinctions.
-- ¬ß Again exactly 4 cases, by the same 2√ó2 argument.
AD-map-interpret : (d‚āĀ d‚āā : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí EndoCase ‚Üí (S d‚āĀ ‚Üí S d‚āā)
AD-map-interpret d‚āĀ d‚āā case-constL _ = ad-‚Ąď d‚āā
AD-map-interpret d‚āĀ d‚āā case-constR _ = ad-r d‚āā
AD-map-interpret d‚āĀ d‚āā case-id     x with ad-cover d‚āĀ x
... | inj‚āĀ _ = ad-‚Ąď d‚āā
... | inj‚āā _ = ad-r d‚āā
AD-map-interpret d‚āĀ d‚āā case-dual   x with ad-cover d‚āĀ x
... | inj‚āĀ _ = ad-r d‚āā
... | inj‚āā _ = ad-‚Ąď d‚āā

AD-map-classify : (d‚āĀ d‚āā : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí (S d‚āĀ ‚Üí S d‚āā) ‚Üí EndoCase
AD-map-classify d‚āĀ d‚āā f with ad-cover d‚āā (f (ad-‚Ąď d‚āĀ)) | ad-cover d‚āā (f (ad-r d‚āĀ))
... | inj‚āĀ _ | inj‚āĀ _ = case-constL
... | inj‚āā _ | inj‚āā _ = case-constR
... | inj‚āĀ _ | inj‚āā _ = case-id
... | inj‚āā _ | inj‚āĀ _ = case-dual

-- ¬ß Soundness: For any map f, interpret(classify f) ‚Č° f pointwise.
AD-map-determined : (d‚āĀ d‚āā : AbstractDistinction) ‚Üí
                    (f g : S d‚āĀ ‚Üí S d‚āā) ‚Üí
                    f (ad-‚Ąď d‚āĀ) ‚Č° g (ad-‚Ąď d‚āĀ) ‚Üí
                    f (ad-r d‚āĀ) ‚Č° g (ad-r d‚āĀ) ‚Üí
                    (x : S d‚āĀ) ‚Üí f x ‚Č° g x
AD-map-determined d‚āĀ d‚āā f g eq‚Ąď eqr x = AD-determined d‚āĀ f g eq‚Ąď eqr x

-- ¬ß Ternary relations reduce to sequential binary distinctions.
-- ¬ß A ternary distinction R(a,b,c) decomposes into:
-- ¬ß step 1: distinguish a from b  (binary)
-- ¬ß step 2: distinguish {a,b} from c  (binary)
-- ¬ß This is forced by the structure of D‚āĀ, which has a single field.

record NoForcingForD‚āĄ : Set where
  field
    all-K4-edges-captured : (e : K4EdgeForStability) ‚Üí K4EdgeCaptured e
    edge-count-complete : edgeCountK4 ‚Č° 6
    algebraic-cardinality : EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-dual ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))
    -- ¬ß ^ The fourth case is the last: Fin4 is exhausted.

theorem-no-D‚āĄ : NoForcingForD‚āĄ
theorem-no-D‚āĄ = record
  { all-K4-edges-captured = theorem-K4-all-edges-captured
  ; edge-count-complete = refl
  ; algebraic-cardinality = refl
  }


-- ¬ß FOUNDATION

record K4UniquenessProof : Set where
  field
    K4-stable     : (e : K4EdgeForStability) ‚Üí K4EdgeCaptured e
    K3-unstable   : K3Edge
    no-forcing-K5 : NoForcingForD‚āĄ
    endo-bijection : (c : EndoCase) ‚Üí Fin4-to-EndoCase (EndoCase-to-Fin4 c) ‚Č° c
    -- ¬ß ^ Exactly four, witnessed by roundtrip

theorem-K4-is-unique : K4UniquenessProof
theorem-K4-is-unique = record
  { K3-unstable = K3-has-uncaptured-edge
  ; K4-stable = theorem-K4-all-edges-captured
  ; no-forcing-K5 = theorem-no-D‚āĄ
  ; endo-bijection = EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ
  }

private
  K4-V : ‚Ąē
  K4-V = vertexCountK4

  K4-E : ‚Ąē
  K4-E = edgeCountK4

  K4-F : ‚Ąē
  K4-F = faceCountK4

  K4-deg : ‚Ąē
  K4-deg = degree-K4

  K4-chi : ‚Ąē
  K4-chi = eulerChar-computed


-- ¬ß CONTINUUM


record K4Lattice : Set where
  field
    scale : LatticeScale
    num-cells : ‚Ąē

log10-electron-planck-ratio : ‚Ąē
log10-electron-planck-ratio = hierarchy-exponent

-- ¬ß LIE-ALGEBRA

data QuatBasis : Set where
  q1 qi qj qk : QuatBasis

quat-basis-count : ‚Ąē
quat-basis-count = 4

theorem-quat-has-4 : quat-basis-count ‚Č° vertexCountK4
theorem-quat-has-4 = refl

data MultSign : Set where
  pos neg : MultSign

quat-mult-sign : QuatBasis ‚Üí QuatBasis ‚Üí MultSign
quat-mult-sign q1 _  = pos
quat-mult-sign _  q1 = pos
-- ¬ß i¬≤ = -1
quat-mult-sign qi qi = neg
-- ¬ß ij = +k
quat-mult-sign qi qj = pos
-- ¬ß ik = -j
quat-mult-sign qi qk = neg
-- ¬ß ji = -k
quat-mult-sign qj qi = neg
-- ¬ß j¬≤ = -1
quat-mult-sign qj qj = neg
-- ¬ß jk = +i
quat-mult-sign qj qk = pos
-- ¬ß ki = +j
quat-mult-sign qk qi = pos
-- ¬ß kj = -i
quat-mult-sign qk qj = neg
-- ¬ß k¬≤ = -1
quat-mult-sign qk qk = neg

-- ¬ß Count of imaginary units = degree of K‚āĄ
quat-imaginary-count : ‚Ąē
quat-imaginary-count = 3

theorem-imaginary-is-degree : quat-imaginary-count ‚Č° degree-K4
theorem-imaginary-is-degree = refl

-- ¬ß Dimension doubling
cd-double : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
cd-double n = n + n

-- ¬ß Quaternions (4) ‚Üí Octonions (8)
theorem-cd-quat-to-oct : cd-double quat-basis-count ‚Č° 8
theorem-cd-quat-to-oct = refl

-- ¬ß Octonion basis: 8 elements from Cayley-Dickson doubling
data OctBasis : Set where
  -- ¬ß Original quaternion copy: {1, i, j, k}
  o1 oi oj ok : OctBasis
  -- ¬ß New elements from doubling: {e, ie, je, ke}
  oe oie oje oke : OctBasis

oct-basis-count : ‚Ąē
oct-basis-count = 8

theorem-oct-has-8 : oct-basis-count ‚Č° cd-double quat-basis-count
theorem-oct-has-8 = refl

-- ¬ß 7 imaginary units (all except real unit o1)
oct-imaginary-count : ‚Ąē
oct-imaginary-count = oct-basis-count ‚ął 1

theorem-oct-7-imaginary : oct-imaginary-count ‚Č° 7
theorem-oct-7-imaginary = refl

-- ¬ß The bridge record: every step is forced
record CayleyDicksonBridge : Set where
  field
    -- ¬ß K‚āĄ has 4 vertices = quaternion basis count
    k4-is-quaternion    : vertexCountK4 ‚Č° quat-basis-count
    -- ¬ß Cayley-Dickson doubles: 4 ‚Üí 8
    cd-doubling         : cd-double quat-basis-count ‚Č° oct-basis-count
    -- ¬ß Octonions have 7 imaginary units
    seven-imaginary     : oct-imaginary-count ‚Č° 7
    -- ¬ß Total dimensionality: 4 (spacetime) + 7 (internal) = 11
    total-11d           : vertexCountK4 + oct-imaginary-count ‚Č° 11

theorem-cayley-dickson-bridge : CayleyDicksonBridge
theorem-cayley-dickson-bridge = record
  { k4-is-quaternion  = refl
  ; cd-doubling       = refl
  ; seven-imaginary   = refl
  ; total-11d         = refl
  }

-- ¬ß Binomial coefficient C(n,2) = n(n-1)/2
-- ¬ß This counts 2-element subsets (pairs) from n elements.
-- ¬ß For graphs: C(n,2) = edges of complete graph K_n.

-- ¬ß C(4,2) = 6: pairs among all quaternion elements ‚Üí edges of K‚āĄ
quat-all-pairs : ‚Ąē
quat-all-pairs = (quat-basis-count * (quat-basis-count ‚ął 1)) div‚Ąē 2

theorem-quat-6-pairs : quat-all-pairs ‚Č° edgeCountK4
theorem-quat-6-pairs = refl

-- ¬ß C(7,2) = 21: pairs among octonion imaginaries
oct-pairs : ‚Ąē
oct-pairs = (oct-imaginary-count * (oct-imaginary-count ‚ął 1)) div‚Ąē 2

theorem-oct-21-pairs : oct-pairs ‚Č° 21
theorem-oct-21-pairs = refl

-- ¬ß Region decomposition of 21 pairs
-- ¬ß C(3,2) = 3
region-original : ‚Ąē
region-original = (3 * 2) div‚Ąē 2

-- ¬ß C(4,2) = 6
region-new : ‚Ąē
region-new = (4 * 3) div‚Ąē 2

-- ¬ß 3 √ó 4 = 12
region-mixed : ‚Ąē
region-mixed = 3 * 4

theorem-regions-sum : region-original + region-new + region-mixed ‚Č° oct-pairs
theorem-regions-sum = refl

-- ¬ß The TCS (Twisted Connected Sum) decomposition:
-- ¬ß 21 pairs split into two blocks from the doubling asymmetry

b‚āā-block-1 : ‚Ąē
b‚āā-block-1 = 11

b‚āā-block-2 : ‚Ąē
b‚āā-block-2 = 10

theorem-tcs-split : b‚āā-block-1 + b‚āā-block-2 ‚Č° oct-pairs
theorem-tcs-split = refl

-- ¬ß From K‚āĄ: three degenerate eigenvalues (proven in spectral theory chapter)
generations-from-K4 : ‚Ąē
generations-from-K4 = degree-K4

-- ¬ß From octonion structure: 21 pairs / 7 imaginary units = 3
generations-from-oct : ‚Ąē
generations-from-oct = oct-pairs div‚Ąē oct-imaginary-count

-- ¬ß Both paths yield the same answer
theorem-generations-agree : generations-from-K4 ‚Č° generations-from-oct
theorem-generations-agree = refl

-- ¬ß And that answer is 3
theorem-three-gen-from-bridge : generations-from-K4 ‚Č° 3
theorem-three-gen-from-bridge = refl

record ‚Ąā : Set where
  constructor _+i_
  field
    re : ‚Ąö
    im : ‚Ąö

open ‚Ąā public

0‚Ąā : ‚Ąā
0‚Ąā = 0‚Ąö +i 0‚Ąö

1‚Ąā : ‚Ąā
1‚Ąā = 1‚Ąö +i 0‚Ąö

i‚Ąā : ‚Ąā
i‚Ąā = 0‚Ąö +i 1‚Ąö

_+‚Ąā_ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
(a +i b) +‚Ąā (c +i d) = (a +‚Ąö c) +i (b +‚Ąö d)

_*‚Ąā_ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
(a +i b) *‚Ąā (c +i d) = (a *‚Ąö c -‚Ąö b *‚Ąö d) +i (a *‚Ąö d +‚Ąö b *‚Ąö c)

conj : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
conj (a +i b) = a +i (-‚Ąö b)

norm¬≤ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąö
norm¬≤ (a +i b) = a *‚Ąö a +‚Ąö b *‚Ąö b

-‚Ąā_ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
-‚Ąā (a +i b) = (-‚Ąö a) +i (-‚Ąö b)

theorem-i-squared : i‚Ąā *‚Ąā i‚Ąā ‚Č° -‚Ąā 1‚Ąā
theorem-i-squared = refl

theorem-z-conj-z : ‚ąÄ (z : ‚Ąā) ‚Üí re (z *‚Ąā conj z) ‚Č° norm¬≤ z
theorem-z-conj-z (a +i b) = refl

K4StateC : Set
K4StateC = K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąā

K4-basis-C : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4StateC
K4-basis-C v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āÄ _  = 0‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 1‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āĀ _  = 0‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āā v‚āā = 1‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āā _  = 0‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = 1‚Ąā
K4-basis-C v‚āÉ _  = 0‚Ąā

_‚äē‚Ąā_ : K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC
(Ōą ‚äē‚Ąā ŌÜ) v = Ōą v +‚Ąā ŌÜ v

_¬∑‚Ąā_ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC
(c ¬∑‚Ąā Ōą) v = c *‚Ąā Ōą v

total-norm¬≤ : K4StateC ‚Üí ‚Ąö
total-norm¬≤ Ōą = norm¬≤ (Ōą v‚āÄ) +‚Ąö norm¬≤ (Ōą v‚āĀ) +‚Ąö norm¬≤ (Ōą v‚āā) +‚Ąö norm¬≤ (Ōą v‚āÉ)

K4State : Set
K4State = K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē

K4-zero-state : K4State
K4-zero-state _ = zero

K4-basis : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4State
K4-basis v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 1
K4-basis v‚āÄ _  = 0
K4-basis v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 1
K4-basis v‚āĀ _  = 0
K4-basis v‚āā v‚āā = 1
K4-basis v‚āā _  = 0
K4-basis v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = 1
K4-basis v‚āÉ _  = 0

_‚äē‚āõ_ : K4State ‚Üí K4State ‚Üí K4State
(Ōą ‚äē‚āõ ŌÜ) v = Ōą v + ŌÜ v

_¬∑‚āõ_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí K4State ‚Üí K4State
(n ¬∑‚āõ Ōą) v = n * Ōą v

total-amplitude : K4State ‚Üí ‚Ąē
total-amplitude Ōą = Ōą v‚āÄ + Ōą v‚āĀ + Ōą v‚āā + Ōą v‚āÉ

theorem-superposition-comm : ‚ąÄ (Ōą ŌÜ : K4State) (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí
  (Ōą ‚äē‚āõ ŌÜ) v ‚Č° (ŌÜ ‚äē‚āõ Ōą) v
theorem-superposition-comm Ōą ŌÜ v = +-comm (Ōą v) (ŌÜ v)

theorem-zero-identity : ‚ąÄ (Ōą : K4State) (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí
  (Ōą ‚äē‚āõ K4-zero-state) v ‚Č° Ōą v
theorem-zero-identity Ōą v = +-identity ≥ (Ōą v)

theorem-basis-normalized : ‚ąÄ (u : K4Vertex) ‚Üí 
  total-amplitude (K4-basis u) ‚Č° 1
theorem-basis-normalized v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-normalized v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-normalized v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-normalized v‚āÉ = refl


amplitude-squared : K4State ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
amplitude-squared Ōą v = Ōą v * Ōą v

total-squared : K4State ‚Üí ‚Ąē
total-squared Ōą = amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āÄ + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āĀ 
                + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āā + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āÉ

probability : K4State ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąö
probability Ōą v with total-squared Ōą
... | zero    = 0‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ
... | suc n   = mk‚Ą§ (amplitude-squared Ōą v) zero / ‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ (suc n)

theorem-born-normalization : ‚ąÄ (Ōą : K4State) ‚Üí
  amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āÄ + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āĀ 
  + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āā + amplitude-squared Ōą v‚āÉ 
  ‚Č° total-squared Ōą
theorem-born-normalization Ōą = refl

theorem-basis-probability : ‚ąÄ (u : K4Vertex) ‚Üí
  total-squared (K4-basis u) ‚Č° 1
theorem-basis-probability v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-probability v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-probability v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-probability v‚āÉ = refl

őī : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
őī v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 1
őī v‚āÄ _  = 0
őī v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 1
őī v‚āĀ _  = 0
őī v‚āā v‚āā = 1
őī v‚āā _  = 0
őī v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = 1
őī v‚āÉ _  = 0

collapse-to : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4State
collapse-to chosen = K4-basis chosen

record ExactHierarchyFormula : Set where
  field
    v-is-4 : K4-V ‚Č° 4
    e-is-6 : K4-E ‚Č° 6
    chi-is-2 : K4-chi ‚Č° 2
    omega-approx : ‚Ąö
    discrete-term : ‚Ąē
    discrete-is-VE-minus-chi : discrete-term ‚Č° K4-V * K4-E ‚ął K4-chi
    discrete-equals-22 : discrete-term ‚Č° 22
    continuum-omega-over-V : ‚Ąö
    continuum-one-over-VplusE : ‚Ąö
    total-integer-part : ‚Ąē
    total-integer-is-22 : total-integer-part ‚Č° 22
    omega-argument-from-k4 : K4-V ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3

theorem-exact-hierarchy : ExactHierarchyFormula
theorem-exact-hierarchy = record
  { v-is-4 = refl
  ; e-is-6 = refl
  ; chi-is-2 = refl
  ; omega-approx = tetrahedron-solid-angle
  ; discrete-term = hierarchy-exponent
  ; discrete-is-VE-minus-chi = refl
  ; discrete-equals-22 = refl
  ; continuum-omega-over-V = (mk‚Ą§ 4777 zero) / (‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 10000)
  ; continuum-one-over-VplusE = (mk‚Ą§ 1 zero) / (‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 10)
  ; total-integer-part = hierarchy-exponent
  ; total-integer-is-22 = refl
  ; omega-argument-from-k4 = refl
  }

record DiscreteContEquivalence : Set where
  field
    graph-vertices : vertexCountK4 ‚Č° 4
    graph-edges : edgeCountK4 ‚Č° 6
    graph-euler : eulerChar-computed ‚Č° 2
    discrete-contribution : hierarchy-exponent ‚Č° 22
    solid-angle-argument : K4-V ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3
    continuum-contribution : ‚Ąö

theorem-discrete-cont-equivalence : DiscreteContEquivalence
theorem-discrete-cont-equivalence = record
  { graph-vertices = refl
  ; graph-edges = refl
  ; graph-euler = refl
  ; discrete-contribution = refl
  ; solid-angle-argument = refl
  ; continuum-contribution = (mk‚Ą§ 3777 zero) / (‚Ąē-to-‚Ąē‚Āļ 10000)
  }


-- ¬ß K4-GRAPH

record K4Consistency : Set where
  field
    vertex-count     : K4-V ‚Č° 4
    edge-count       : K4-E ‚Č° 6
    all-captured     : (e : K4EdgeForStability) ‚Üí K4EdgeCaptured e
    euler-is-2       : K4-chi ‚Č° 2

theorem-K4-consistency : K4Consistency
theorem-K4-consistency = record
  { vertex-count = refl
  ; edge-count   = refl
  ; all-captured = theorem-K4-all-edges-captured
  ; euler-is-2   = refl
  }

K2-vertex-count : ‚Ąē
K2-vertex-count = K4-V ‚ął 2


theorem-K2-insufficient : suc K2-vertex-count ‚Č§ K4-V
theorem-K2-insufficient = s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s z‚Č§n))

K3-vertex-count : ‚Ąē
K3-vertex-count = K4-V ‚ął 1

K3-edge-count-val : ‚Ąē
K3-edge-count-val = (K3-vertex-count * (K3-vertex-count ‚ął 1)) div‚Ąē 2

K5-vertex-count : ‚Ąē
K5-vertex-count = suc K4-V

K5-edge-count : ‚Ąē
K5-edge-count = (K5-vertex-count * (K5-vertex-count ‚ął 1)) div‚Ąē 2

theorem-K5-unreachable : NoForcingForD‚āĄ
theorem-K5-unreachable = theorem-no-D‚āĄ

record K4Exclusivity-Graph : Set where
  field
    K2-too-small    : suc K2-vertex-count ‚Č§ K4-V
    K3-uncaptured   : K3Edge
    K4-all-captured : (e : K4EdgeForStability) ‚Üí K4EdgeCaptured e
    K5-no-forcing   : NoForcingForD‚āĄ

theorem-K4-exclusivity-graph : K4Exclusivity-Graph
theorem-K4-exclusivity-graph = record
  { K2-too-small    = theorem-K2-insufficient
  ; K3-uncaptured   = K3-has-uncaptured-edge
  ; K4-all-captured = theorem-K4-all-edges-captured
  ; K5-no-forcing   = theorem-no-D‚āĄ
  }

theorem-K4-edges-forced : K4-V * (K4-V ‚ął 1) ‚Č° 12
theorem-K4-edges-forced = refl

theorem-K4-degree-forced : K4-V ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3
theorem-K4-degree-forced = refl

record K4Robustness : Set where
  field
    V-is-forced       : K4-V ‚Č° 4
    E-is-forced       : K4-E ‚Č° 6
    deg-is-forced     : K4-V ‚ął 1 ‚Č° 3
    chi-is-forced     : K4-chi ‚Č° 2
    K3-fails          : K3Edge
    K5-fails          : NoForcingForD‚āĄ

theorem-K4-robustness : K4Robustness
theorem-K4-robustness = record
  { V-is-forced   = refl
  ; E-is-forced   = refl
  ; deg-is-forced = refl
  ; chi-is-forced = refl
  ; K3-fails      = K3-has-uncaptured-edge
  ; K5-fails      = theorem-no-D‚āĄ
  }

record K4CrossConstraints : Set where
  field
    complete-graph-formula : K4-E * 2 ‚Č° K4-V * (K4-V ‚ął 1)
    
    euler-formula          : (K4-V + K4-F) ‚Č° K4-E + K4-chi
    
    degree-formula         : K4-deg ‚Č° K4-V ‚ął 1

theorem-K4-cross-constraints : K4CrossConstraints
theorem-K4-cross-constraints = record
  { complete-graph-formula = refl
  ; euler-formula          = refl
  ; degree-formula         = refl
  }

record K4StructuralConsistency : Set where
  field
    consistency       : K4Consistency
    exclusivity       : K4Exclusivity-Graph
    robustness        : K4Robustness
    cross-constraints : K4CrossConstraints

lemma-K4-structural-consistency : K4StructuralConsistency
lemma-K4-structural-consistency = record
  { consistency       = theorem-K4-consistency
  ; exclusivity       = theorem-K4-exclusivity-graph
  ; robustness        = theorem-K4-robustness
  ; cross-constraints = theorem-K4-cross-constraints
  }

K4UniquenessComplete : Set
K4UniquenessComplete = K4StructuralConsistency

theorem-K4-uniqueness-complete : K4UniquenessComplete
theorem-K4-uniqueness-complete = lemma-K4-structural-consistency

record K4Edge : Set where
  constructor mkEdge
  field
    src      : K4Vertex
    tgt      : K4Vertex
    distinct : vertex-to-id src ‚ČĘ vertex-to-id tgt

edge-01 edge-02 edge-03 edge-12 edge-13 edge-23 : K4Edge
edge-01 = mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āĀ D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āĀ-id
edge-02 = mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āā D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āā-id
edge-03 = mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āÉ D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id
edge-12 = mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āā D‚āĀ-id‚ČĘD‚āā-id
edge-13 = mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āÉ D‚āĀ-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id
edge-23 = mkEdge v‚āā v‚āÉ D‚āā-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id

K4-is-complete : (v w : K4Vertex) ‚Üí ¬¨ (vertex-to-id v ‚Č° vertex-to-id w) ‚Üí 
                 (K4Edge ‚äé K4Edge)
K4-is-complete v‚āÄ v‚āÄ neq = ‚ä•-elim (neq refl)
K4-is-complete v‚āÄ v‚āĀ _   = inj‚āĀ edge-01
K4-is-complete v‚āÄ v‚āā _   = inj‚āĀ edge-02
K4-is-complete v‚āÄ v‚āÉ _   = inj‚āĀ edge-03
K4-is-complete v‚āĀ v‚āÄ _   = inj‚āā edge-01
K4-is-complete v‚āĀ v‚āĀ neq = ‚ä•-elim (neq refl)
K4-is-complete v‚āĀ v‚āā _   = inj‚āĀ edge-12
K4-is-complete v‚āĀ v‚āÉ _   = inj‚āĀ edge-13
K4-is-complete v‚āā v‚āÄ _   = inj‚āā edge-02
K4-is-complete v‚āā v‚āĀ _   = inj‚āā edge-12
K4-is-complete v‚āā v‚āā neq = ‚ä•-elim (neq refl)
K4-is-complete v‚āā v‚āÉ _   = inj‚āĀ edge-23
K4-is-complete v‚āÉ v‚āÄ _   = inj‚āā edge-03
K4-is-complete v‚āÉ v‚āĀ _   = inj‚āā edge-13
K4-is-complete v‚āÉ v‚āā _   = inj‚āā edge-23
K4-is-complete v‚āÉ v‚āÉ neq = ‚ä•-elim (neq refl)

k4-edge-count : ‚Ąē
k4-edge-count = K4-E

theorem-k4-has-6-edges : k4-edge-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))
theorem-k4-has-6-edges = refl

genesis-to-vertex : GenesisID ‚Üí K4Vertex
genesis-to-vertex D‚āÄ-id = v‚āÄ
genesis-to-vertex D‚āĀ-id = v‚āĀ
genesis-to-vertex D‚āā-id = v‚āā
genesis-to-vertex D‚āÉ-id = v‚āÉ

vertex-to-genesis : K4Vertex ‚Üí GenesisID
vertex-to-genesis v‚āÄ = D‚āÄ-id
vertex-to-genesis v‚āĀ = D‚āĀ-id
vertex-to-genesis v‚āā = D‚āā-id
vertex-to-genesis v‚āÉ = D‚āÉ-id

theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1 : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí genesis-to-vertex (vertex-to-genesis v) ‚Č° v
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1 v‚āā = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2 : ‚ąÄ (d : GenesisID) ‚Üí vertex-to-genesis (genesis-to-vertex d) ‚Č° d
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2 D‚āÄ-id = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2 D‚āĀ-id = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2 D‚āā-id = refl
theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2 D‚āÉ-id = refl

record VertexGenesisBijection : Set where
  field
    to-vertex : GenesisID ‚Üí K4Vertex
    to-genesis : K4Vertex ‚Üí GenesisID
    iso-1 : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí to-vertex (to-genesis v) ‚Č° v
    iso-2 : ‚ąÄ (d : GenesisID) ‚Üí to-genesis (to-vertex d) ‚Č° d

theorem-vertices-are-genesis : VertexGenesisBijection
theorem-vertices-are-genesis = record
  { to-vertex = genesis-to-vertex
  ; to-genesis = vertex-to-genesis
  ; iso-1 = theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-1
  ; iso-2 = theorem-vertex-genesis-iso-2
  }


-- ¬ß FOUNDATION

data GenesisPairIsDistinct : GenesisID ‚Üí GenesisID ‚Üí Set where
  dist-01 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÄ-id D‚āĀ-id
  dist-02 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÄ-id D‚āā-id
  dist-03 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÄ-id D‚āÉ-id
  dist-10 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āĀ-id D‚āÄ-id
  dist-12 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āĀ-id D‚āā-id
  dist-13 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āĀ-id D‚āÉ-id
  dist-20 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āā-id D‚āÄ-id
  dist-21 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āā-id D‚āĀ-id
  dist-23 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āā-id D‚āÉ-id
  dist-30 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÉ-id D‚āÄ-id
  dist-31 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÉ-id D‚āĀ-id
  dist-32 : GenesisPairIsDistinct D‚āÉ-id D‚āā-id

genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct : ‚ąÄ {d‚āĀ d‚āā} ‚Üí GenesisPairIsDistinct d‚āĀ d‚āā ‚Üí 
  vertex-to-id (genesis-to-vertex d‚āĀ) ‚ČĘ vertex-to-id (genesis-to-vertex d‚āā)
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-01 = D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āĀ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-02 = D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āā-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-03 = D‚āÄ-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-10 = D‚āĀ-id‚ČĘD‚āÄ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-12 = D‚āĀ-id‚ČĘD‚āā-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-13 = D‚āĀ-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-20 = D‚āā-id‚ČĘD‚āÄ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-21 = D‚āā-id‚ČĘD‚āĀ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-23 = D‚āā-id‚ČĘD‚āÉ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-30 = D‚āÉ-id‚ČĘD‚āÄ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-31 = D‚āÉ-id‚ČĘD‚āĀ-id
genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct dist-32 = D‚āÉ-id‚ČĘD‚āā-id

genesis-pair-to-edge : ‚ąÄ (d‚āĀ d‚āā : GenesisID) ‚Üí GenesisPairIsDistinct d‚āĀ d‚āā ‚Üí K4Edge
genesis-pair-to-edge d‚āĀ d‚āā prf = 
  mkEdge (genesis-to-vertex d‚āĀ) (genesis-to-vertex d‚āā) (genesis-distinct-to-vertex-distinct prf)

edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct : ‚ąÄ (e : K4Edge) ‚Üí 
  GenesisPairIsDistinct (vertex-to-genesis (K4Edge.src e)) (vertex-to-genesis (K4Edge.tgt e))
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āÄ prf) = ‚ä•-elim (prf refl)
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āĀ _) = dist-01
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āā _) = dist-02
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÄ v‚āÉ _) = dist-03
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āÄ _) = dist-10
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āĀ prf) = ‚ä•-elim (prf refl)
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āā _) = dist-12
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āĀ v‚āÉ _) = dist-13
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āā v‚āÄ _) = dist-20
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āā v‚āĀ _) = dist-21
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āā v‚āā prf) = ‚ä•-elim (prf refl)
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āā v‚āÉ _) = dist-23
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÉ v‚āÄ _) = dist-30
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÉ v‚āĀ _) = dist-31
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÉ v‚āā _) = dist-32
edge-to-genesis-pair-distinct (mkEdge v‚āÉ v‚āÉ prf) = ‚ä•-elim (prf refl)

distinct-genesis-pairs-count : ‚Ąē
distinct-genesis-pairs-count = K4-E

theorem-6-distinct-pairs : distinct-genesis-pairs-count ‚Č° 6
theorem-6-distinct-pairs = refl

data EdgeStatus : Set where
  was-new-irreducible : EdgeStatus
  was-already-exists  : EdgeStatus

classify-edge-by-vertices : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí EdgeStatus
classify-edge-by-vertices v‚āÄ v‚āā = was-new-irreducible
classify-edge-by-vertices v‚āā v‚āÄ = was-new-irreducible
classify-edge-by-vertices _ _ = was-already-exists

edge-classification : K4Edge ‚Üí EdgeStatus
edge-classification (mkEdge src tgt _) = classify-edge-by-vertices src tgt

theorem-K4-forced-by-irreducible-pair : 
  classify-pair D‚āÄ-id D‚āā-id ‚Č° new-irreducible ‚Üí
  k4-edge-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))
theorem-K4-forced-by-irreducible-pair _ = theorem-k4-has-6-edges

_‚Čü-vertex_ : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí Bool
v‚āÄ ‚Čü-vertex v‚āÄ = true
v‚āĀ ‚Čü-vertex v‚āĀ = true
v‚āā ‚Čü-vertex v‚āā = true
v‚āÉ ‚Čü-vertex v‚āÉ = true
_  ‚Čü-vertex _  = false

Adjacency : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
Adjacency i j with i ‚Čü-vertex j
... | true  = zero
... | false = suc zero

theorem-adjacency-symmetric : ‚ąÄ (i j : K4Vertex) ‚Üí Adjacency i j ‚Č° Adjacency j i
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āā = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āā = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āā v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āā v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āā v‚āā = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āā v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āā = refl
theorem-adjacency-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = refl

Degree : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
Degree v = Adjacency v v‚āÄ + (Adjacency v v‚āĀ + (Adjacency v v‚āā + Adjacency v v‚āÉ))

theorem-degree-3 : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí Degree v ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))
theorem-degree-3 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-degree-3 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-degree-3 v‚āā = refl
theorem-degree-3 v‚āÉ = refl

DegreeMatrix : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
DegreeMatrix i j with i ‚Čü-vertex j
... | true  = Degree i
... | false = zero

natTo‚Ą§ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ą§
natTo‚Ą§ n = mk‚Ą§ n zero

Laplacian : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
Laplacian i j = natTo‚Ą§ (DegreeMatrix i j) +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (natTo‚Ą§ (Adjacency i j))






theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āÄv‚āā : Laplacian v‚āÄ v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ zero (suc zero)
theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āÄv‚āā = refl

theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āÄv‚āÉ : Laplacian v‚āÄ v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ zero (suc zero)
theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āÄv‚āÉ = refl


theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āĀv‚āÉ : Laplacian v‚āĀ v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ zero (suc zero)
theorem-laplacian-offdiag-v‚āĀv‚āÉ = refl









theorem-L-symmetric : ‚ąÄ (i j : K4Vertex) ‚Üí Laplacian i j ‚Č° Laplacian j i
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āā = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÄ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āā = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āĀ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āā v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āā v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āā v‚āā = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āā v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āā = refl
theorem-L-symmetric v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = refl

Eigenvector : Set
Eigenvector = K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§

applyLaplacian : Eigenvector ‚Üí Eigenvector
applyLaplacian ev = őĽ v ‚Üí 
  ((Laplacian v v‚āÄ *‚Ą§ ev v‚āÄ) +‚Ą§ (Laplacian v v‚āĀ *‚Ą§ ev v‚āĀ)) +‚Ą§ 
  ((Laplacian v v‚āā *‚Ą§ ev v‚āā) +‚Ą§ (Laplacian v v‚āÉ *‚Ą§ ev v‚āÉ))

scaleEigenvector : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí Eigenvector ‚Üí Eigenvector
scaleEigenvector scalar ev = őĽ v ‚Üí scalar *‚Ą§ ev v

őĽ‚āĄ : ‚Ą§
őĽ‚āĄ = mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) zero

eigenvector-1 : Eigenvector
eigenvector-1 v‚āÄ = 1‚Ą§
eigenvector-1 v‚āĀ = -1‚Ą§
eigenvector-1 v‚āā = 0‚Ą§
eigenvector-1 v‚āÉ = 0‚Ą§

eigenvector-2 : Eigenvector
eigenvector-2 v‚āÄ = 1‚Ą§
eigenvector-2 v‚āĀ = 0‚Ą§
eigenvector-2 v‚āā = -1‚Ą§
eigenvector-2 v‚āÉ = 0‚Ą§

eigenvector-3 : Eigenvector
eigenvector-3 v‚āÄ = 1‚Ą§
eigenvector-3 v‚āĀ = 0‚Ą§
eigenvector-3 v‚āā = 0‚Ą§
eigenvector-3 v‚āÉ = -1‚Ą§

IsEigenvector : Eigenvector ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí Set
IsEigenvector ev eigenval = ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí 
  applyLaplacian ev v ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector eigenval ev v

theorem-eigenvector-1 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-1 őĽ‚āĄ
theorem-eigenvector-1 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-1 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-1 v‚āā = refl
theorem-eigenvector-1 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-eigenvector-2 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-2 őĽ‚āĄ
theorem-eigenvector-2 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-2 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-2 v‚āā = refl
theorem-eigenvector-2 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-eigenvector-3 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-3 őĽ‚āĄ
theorem-eigenvector-3 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-3 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-eigenvector-3 v‚āā = refl
theorem-eigenvector-3 v‚āÉ = refl


-- ¬ß ARITHMETIC

record EigenspaceConsistency : Set where
  field
    ev1-satisfies : IsEigenvector eigenvector-1 őĽ‚āĄ
    ev2-satisfies : IsEigenvector eigenvector-2 őĽ‚āĄ
    ev3-satisfies : IsEigenvector eigenvector-3 őĽ‚āĄ

theorem-eigenspace-consistent : EigenspaceConsistency
theorem-eigenspace-consistent = record
  { ev1-satisfies = theorem-eigenvector-1
  ; ev2-satisfies = theorem-eigenvector-2
  ; ev3-satisfies = theorem-eigenvector-3
  }

dot-product : Eigenvector ‚Üí Eigenvector ‚Üí ‚Ą§
dot-product ev1 ev2 = 
  (ev1 v‚āÄ *‚Ą§ ev2 v‚āÄ) +‚Ą§ ((ev1 v‚āĀ *‚Ą§ ev2 v‚āĀ) +‚Ą§ ((ev1 v‚āā *‚Ą§ ev2 v‚āā) +‚Ą§ (ev1 v‚āÉ *‚Ą§ ev2 v‚āÉ)))

det2x2 : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
det2x2 a b c d = (a *‚Ą§ d) +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (b *‚Ą§ c)

det3x3 : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
det3x3 a‚āĀ‚āĀ a‚āĀ‚āā a‚āĀ‚āÉ a‚āā‚āĀ a‚āā‚āā a‚āā‚āÉ a‚āÉ‚āĀ a‚āÉ‚āā a‚āÉ‚āÉ =
  let minor1 = det2x2 a‚āā‚āā a‚āā‚āÉ a‚āÉ‚āā a‚āÉ‚āÉ
      minor2 = det2x2 a‚āā‚āĀ a‚āā‚āÉ a‚āÉ‚āĀ a‚āÉ‚āÉ
      minor3 = det2x2 a‚āā‚āĀ a‚āā‚āā a‚āÉ‚āĀ a‚āÉ‚āā
  in (a‚āĀ‚āĀ *‚Ą§ minor1 +‚Ą§ (neg‚Ą§ (a‚āĀ‚āā *‚Ą§ minor2))) +‚Ą§ a‚āĀ‚āÉ *‚Ą§ minor3

det-eigenvectors : ‚Ą§
det-eigenvectors = det3x3 
  1‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§
  -1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
  0‚Ą§ -1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§

theorem-K4-linear-independence : det-eigenvectors ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-K4-linear-independence = refl

K4-eigenvectors-nonzero-det : det-eigenvectors ‚Č° 0‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚ä•
K4-eigenvectors-nonzero-det ()

record EigenspaceExclusivity : Set where
  field
    determinant-nonzero : ¬¨ (det-eigenvectors ‚Č° 0‚Ą§)
    determinant-value   : det-eigenvectors ‚Č° 1‚Ą§

theorem-eigenspace-exclusive : EigenspaceExclusivity
theorem-eigenspace-exclusive = record
  { determinant-nonzero = K4-eigenvectors-nonzero-det
  ; determinant-value = theorem-K4-linear-independence
  }

norm-squared : Eigenvector ‚Üí ‚Ą§
norm-squared ev = dot-product ev ev

theorem-ev1-norm : norm-squared eigenvector-1 ‚Č° mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-ev1-norm = refl

theorem-ev2-norm : norm-squared eigenvector-2 ‚Č° mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-ev2-norm = refl

theorem-ev3-norm : norm-squared eigenvector-3 ‚Č° mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-ev3-norm = refl

record EigenspaceRobustness : Set where
  field
    ev1-nonzero : ¬¨ (norm-squared eigenvector-1 ‚Č° 0‚Ą§)
    ev2-nonzero : ¬¨ (norm-squared eigenvector-2 ‚Č° 0‚Ą§)
    ev3-nonzero : ¬¨ (norm-squared eigenvector-3 ‚Č° 0‚Ą§)

theorem-eigenspace-robust : EigenspaceRobustness
theorem-eigenspace-robust = record
  { ev1-nonzero = őĽ ()
  ; ev2-nonzero = őĽ ()
  ; ev3-nonzero = őĽ ()
  }

theorem-eigenvalue-multiplicity-3 : ‚Ąē
theorem-eigenvalue-multiplicity-3 = suc (suc (suc zero))

record Mat3‚Ą§ : Set where
  constructor mat3
  field
    r‚āĀ‚āĀ r‚āĀ‚āā r‚āĀ‚āÉ r‚āā‚āĀ r‚āā‚āā r‚āā‚āÉ r‚āÉ‚āĀ r‚āÉ‚āā r‚āÉ‚āÉ : ‚Ą§

det3 : Mat3‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
det3 (mat3 a b c d e f g h k) = det3x3 a b c d e f g h k

I‚āÉ‚Ą§ : Mat3‚Ą§
I‚āÉ‚Ą§ = mat3 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§

theorem-det-I‚āÉ : det3 I‚āÉ‚Ą§ ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-I‚āÉ = refl

ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 : Mat3‚Ą§
ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 = mat3 (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)
              0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§
              0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§

theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 ‚Č° neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 = refl

ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 : Mat3‚Ą§
ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 = mat3 0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§
                 (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)
                  0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§

theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 = refl

ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx : Mat3‚Ą§
ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx = mat3 (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)
              0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§
              0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§

ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy : Mat3‚Ą§
ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy = mat3  0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§
             (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)
              1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§

ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz : Mat3‚Ą§
ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz = mat3  0‚Ą§          1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§
               1‚Ą§          0‚Ą§          0‚Ą§
             (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§) (neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§)

theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx = refl

theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy = refl

theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-det-ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz = refl

data Reversibility : Set where
  symmetric  : Reversibility
  asymmetric : Reversibility

k4-edge-symmetric : Reversibility
k4-edge-symmetric = symmetric

drift-asymmetric : Reversibility
drift-asymmetric = asymmetric

signature-from-reversibility : Reversibility ‚Üí ‚Ą§
signature-from-reversibility symmetric  = 1‚Ą§
signature-from-reversibility asymmetric = -1‚Ą§

theorem-k4-edges-bidirectional : ‚ąÄ (e : K4Edge) ‚Üí k4-edge-symmetric ‚Č° symmetric
theorem-k4-edges-bidirectional _ = refl

-- ¬ß Vertex count at each genesis step: strictly increasing
genesis-vertices : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
-- ¬ß D‚āÄ alone
genesis-vertices zero = 1
-- ¬ß D‚āÄ, D‚āĀ
genesis-vertices (suc zero) = 2
-- ¬ß D‚āÄ, D‚āĀ, D‚āā
genesis-vertices (suc (suc zero)) = 3
-- ¬ß D‚āÄ, D‚āĀ, D‚āā, D‚āÉ
genesis-vertices (suc (suc (suc _))) = 4

-- ¬ß Each step strictly adds structure: step n < step (n+1) for n ‚ąą {0,1,2}
genesis-monotone-0 : genesis-vertices 0 < genesis-vertices 1
genesis-monotone-0 = s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s z‚Č§n)

genesis-monotone-1 : genesis-vertices 1 < genesis-vertices 2
genesis-monotone-1 = s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s z‚Č§n))

genesis-monotone-2 : genesis-vertices 2 < genesis-vertices 3
genesis-monotone-2 = s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s (s‚Č§s z‚Č§n)))

data SignatureMismatch : Reversibility ‚Üí Reversibility ‚Üí Set where
  space-time-differ : SignatureMismatch symmetric asymmetric

theorem-signature-mismatch : SignatureMismatch k4-edge-symmetric drift-asymmetric
theorem-signature-mismatch = space-time-differ

theorem-spatial-signature : signature-from-reversibility k4-edge-symmetric ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
theorem-spatial-signature = refl

theorem-temporal-signature : signature-from-reversibility drift-asymmetric ‚Č° -1‚Ą§
theorem-temporal-signature = refl

record EigenvectorVerification : Set where
  field
    ev1-at-v‚āÄ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-1 v‚āÄ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-1 v‚āÄ
    ev1-at-v‚āĀ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-1 v‚āĀ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-1 v‚āĀ
    ev1-at-v‚āā : applyLaplacian eigenvector-1 v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-1 v‚āā
    ev1-at-v‚āÉ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-1 v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-1 v‚āÉ
    ev2-at-v‚āÄ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-2 v‚āÄ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-2 v‚āÄ
    ev2-at-v‚āĀ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-2 v‚āĀ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-2 v‚āĀ
    ev2-at-v‚āā : applyLaplacian eigenvector-2 v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-2 v‚āā
    ev2-at-v‚āÉ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-2 v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-2 v‚āÉ
    ev3-at-v‚āÄ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-3 v‚āÄ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-3 v‚āÄ
    ev3-at-v‚āĀ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-3 v‚āĀ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-3 v‚āĀ
    ev3-at-v‚āā : applyLaplacian eigenvector-3 v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-3 v‚āā
    ev3-at-v‚āÉ : applyLaplacian eigenvector-3 v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ scaleEigenvector őĽ‚āĄ eigenvector-3 v‚āÉ

theorem-all-eigenvector-equations : EigenvectorVerification
theorem-all-eigenvector-equations = record
  { ev1-at-v‚āÄ = refl
  ; ev1-at-v‚āĀ = refl
  ; ev1-at-v‚āā = refl
  ; ev1-at-v‚āÉ = refl
  ; ev2-at-v‚āÄ = refl
  ; ev2-at-v‚āĀ = refl
  ; ev2-at-v‚āā = refl
  ; ev2-at-v‚āÉ = refl
  ; ev3-at-v‚āÄ = refl
  ; ev3-at-v‚āĀ = refl
  ; ev3-at-v‚āā = refl
  ; ev3-at-v‚āÉ = refl
  }


record TopologicalMode : Set where
  field
    weight-v‚āÄ : ‚Ąē
    weight-v‚āĀ : ‚Ąē
    weight-v‚āā : ‚Ąē
    weight-v‚āÉ : ‚Ąē
    total-weight : ‚Ąē
    total-weight-def : total-weight ‚Č° 
      weight-v‚āÄ + weight-v‚āĀ + weight-v‚āā + weight-v‚āÉ

mode-from-vector : (K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§) ‚Üí TopologicalMode
mode-from-vector vec = 
  record
    { weight-v‚āÄ = w0
    ; weight-v‚āĀ = w1
    ; weight-v‚āā = w2
    ; weight-v‚āÉ = w3
    ; total-weight = w0 + w1 + w2 + w3
    ; total-weight-def = refl
    }
  where
    le : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Bool
    le zero _ = true
    le (suc _) zero = false
    le (suc m) (suc n) = le m n

    abs-val : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ąē
    abs-val (mk‚Ą§ p n) with le p n
    ... | true  = n ‚ął p
    ... | false = p ‚ął n

    w0 = abs-val (vec v‚āÄ)
    w1 = abs-val (vec v‚āĀ)
    w2 = abs-val (vec v‚āā)
    w3 = abs-val (vec v‚āÉ)

electron-mode : TopologicalMode
electron-mode = mode-from-vector eigenvector-1

ev-sum-2 : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
ev-sum-2 v = eigenvector-1 v +‚Ą§ eigenvector-2 v

muon-mode : TopologicalMode
muon-mode = mode-from-vector ev-sum-2

ev-sum-3 : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
ev-sum-3 v = (eigenvector-1 v +‚Ą§ eigenvector-2 v) +‚Ą§ eigenvector-3 v

tau-mode : TopologicalMode
tau-mode = mode-from-vector ev-sum-3
eigenmode-count-func : TopologicalMode ‚Üí ‚Ąē
eigenmode-count-func m with TopologicalMode.total-weight m
... | 2 = 1
... | 4 = 2
... | 6 = 3
... | _ = 0

axiom-electron-single : eigenmode-count-func electron-mode ‚Č° 1
axiom-electron-single = refl

axiom-muon-double : eigenmode-count-func muon-mode ‚Č° 2
axiom-muon-double = refl

axiom-tau-triple : eigenmode-count-func tau-mode ‚Č° 3
axiom-tau-triple = refl


-- ¬ß DRIFT

data DriftDirection : Set where
  genesis-to-k4 : DriftDirection

theorem-drift-unidirectional : drift-asymmetric ‚Č° asymmetric
theorem-drift-unidirectional = refl


-- ¬ß QUANTUM

record K4QuantumMeasurement : Set where
  field
    pre-state     : K4State
    outcome       : K4Vertex
    post-state    : K4State
    collapse-law  : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí post-state v ‚Č° őī outcome v

measure : K4State ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí K4QuantumMeasurement
measure Ōą choice = record
  { pre-state    = Ōą
  ; outcome      = choice
  ; post-state   = collapse-to choice
  ; collapse-law = őĽ v ‚Üí collapse-basis-is-delta choice v
  }
  where
    collapse-basis-is-delta : ‚ąÄ (c v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí K4-basis c v ‚Č° őī c v
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÄ v‚āā = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÄ v‚āÉ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āĀ v‚āā = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āĀ v‚āÉ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āā v‚āÄ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āā v‚āĀ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āā v‚āā = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āā v‚āÉ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÉ v‚āÄ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÉ v‚āĀ = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÉ v‚āā = refl
    collapse-basis-is-delta v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = refl

adjacent : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
adjacent v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 0
adjacent v‚āÄ _  = 1
adjacent v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 0
adjacent v‚āĀ _  = 1
adjacent v‚āā v‚āā = 0
adjacent v‚āā _  = 1
adjacent v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = 0
adjacent v‚āÉ _  = 1

sum-neighbors : K4State ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
sum-neighbors Ōą v = adjacent v v‚āÄ * Ōą v‚āÄ + adjacent v v‚āĀ * Ōą v‚āĀ
                  + adjacent v v‚āā * Ōą v‚āā + adjacent v v‚āÉ * Ōą v‚āÉ

evolve-step : K4State ‚Üí K4State
evolve-step Ōą v = sum-neighbors Ōą v

evolve-K4 : ‚Ąē ‚Üí K4State ‚Üí K4State
evolve-K4 zero Ōą = Ōą
evolve-K4 (suc n) Ōą = evolve-step (evolve-K4 n Ōą)

theorem-adjacency-degree-3 : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí
  adjacent v v‚āÄ + adjacent v v‚āĀ + adjacent v v‚āā + adjacent v v‚āÉ ‚Č° K4-deg
theorem-adjacency-degree-3 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-adjacency-degree-3 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-adjacency-degree-3 v‚āā = refl
theorem-adjacency-degree-3 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-basis-spreads : ‚ąÄ (u v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí
  evolve-step (K4-basis u) v ‚Č° adjacent v u
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÄ v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÄ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āĀ v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āĀ v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āā v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āā v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āā v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āā v‚āÉ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÉ v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÉ v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÉ v‚āā = refl
theorem-basis-spreads v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = refl

adjacent-C : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 0‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āÄ _  = i‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 0‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āĀ _  = i‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āā v‚āā = 0‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āā _  = i‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āÉ v‚āÉ = 0‚Ąā
adjacent-C v‚āÉ _  = i‚Ąā

sum-neighbors-C : K4StateC ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąā
sum-neighbors-C Ōą v = ((adjacent-C v v‚āÄ *‚Ąā Ōą v‚āÄ) +‚Ąā (adjacent-C v v‚āĀ *‚Ąā Ōą v‚āĀ))
                   +‚Ąā ((adjacent-C v v‚āā *‚Ąā Ōą v‚āā) +‚Ąā (adjacent-C v v‚āÉ *‚Ąā Ōą v‚āÉ))

evolve-step-C : K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC
evolve-step-C Ōą v = sum-neighbors-C Ōą v

evolve-C : ‚Ąē ‚Üí K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC
evolve-C zero Ōą = Ōą
evolve-C (suc n) Ōą = evolve-step-C (evolve-C n Ōą)

plus-state : K4StateC
plus-state v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
plus-state v‚āĀ = 1‚Ąā
plus-state v‚āā = 0‚Ąā
plus-state v‚āÉ = 0‚Ąā

minus-state : K4StateC
minus-state v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
minus-state v‚āĀ = -‚Ąā 1‚Ąā
minus-state v‚āā = 0‚Ąā
minus-state v‚āÉ = 0‚Ąā

normalize‚Ąā : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
normalize‚Ąā (a +i b) = 
  let a' = normalize‚Ą§ (num a)
      b' = normalize‚Ą§ (num b)
  in (a' / den a) +i (b' / den b)

-1‚Ąā-direct : ‚Ąā
-1‚Ąā-direct = (-1‚Ą§ / one‚Āļ) +i 0‚Ąö

minus-state' : K4StateC
minus-state' v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
minus-state' v‚āĀ = -1‚Ąā-direct
minus-state' v‚āā = 0‚Ąā
minus-state' v‚āÉ = 0‚Ąā

doubled-plus : K4StateC
doubled-plus = plus-state ‚äē‚Ąā plus-state

theorem-constructive-v‚āÄ : doubled-plus v‚āÄ ‚Č° (2‚Ąö +i 0‚Ąö)
theorem-constructive-v‚āÄ = refl

theorem-constructive-v‚āĀ : doubled-plus v‚āĀ ‚Č° (2‚Ąö +i 0‚Ąö)
theorem-constructive-v‚āĀ = refl

theorem-plus-minus-differ : plus-state v‚āĀ ‚ČĘ minus-state' v‚āĀ
theorem-plus-minus-differ ()

theorem-norm-plus : norm¬≤ (plus-state v‚āĀ) ‚Č° 1‚Ąö
theorem-norm-plus = refl

theorem-norm-minus : norm¬≤ (minus-state' v‚āĀ) ‚Č° 1‚Ąö
theorem-norm-minus = refl

amplitude-sum-raw : ‚Ąā
amplitude-sum-raw = 1‚Ąā +‚Ąā (-‚Ąā 1‚Ąā)

theorem-destructive-interference : normalize‚Ąā (1‚Ąā +‚Ąā (-‚Ąā 1‚Ąā)) ‚Č° 0‚Ąā
theorem-destructive-interference = refl

theorem-evolution-preserves-vertices : ‚ąÄ (Ōą : K4StateC) (n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí
  (őĽ v ‚Üí evolve-C n Ōą v) ‚Č° evolve-C n Ōą
theorem-evolution-preserves-vertices Ōą n = refl

theorem-evolution-compose : ‚ąÄ (Ōą : K4StateC) (m n : ‚Ąē) ‚Üí
  evolve-C m (evolve-C n Ōą) ‚Č° evolve-C (m + n) Ōą
theorem-evolution-compose Ōą zero    n = refl
theorem-evolution-compose Ōą (suc m) n = cong evolve-step-C (theorem-evolution-compose Ōą m n)

K4√óK4State : Set
K4√óK4State = K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąā

_‚äó_ : K4StateC ‚Üí K4StateC ‚Üí K4√óK4State
(Ōą ‚äó ŌÜ) v w = Ōą v *‚Ąā ŌÜ w

bell-ő¶‚Āļ : K4√óK4State
bell-ő¶‚Āļ v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő¶‚Āļ v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő¶‚Āļ _  _  = 0‚Ąā

bell-ő¶‚ĀĽ : K4√óK4State
bell-ő¶‚ĀĽ v‚āÄ v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő¶‚ĀĽ v‚āĀ v‚āĀ = -‚Ąā 1‚Ąā
bell-ő¶‚ĀĽ _  _  = 0‚Ąā

bell-ő®‚Āļ : K4√óK4State
bell-ő®‚Āļ v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő®‚Āļ v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő®‚Āļ _  _  = 0‚Ąā

bell-ő®‚ĀĽ : K4√óK4State
bell-ő®‚ĀĽ v‚āÄ v‚āĀ = 1‚Ąā
bell-ő®‚ĀĽ v‚āĀ v‚āÄ = -‚Ąā 1‚Ąā
bell-ő®‚ĀĽ _  _  = 0‚Ąā

trace-second : K4√óK4State ‚Üí K4StateC
trace-second ŌĀ v = (ŌĀ v v‚āÄ +‚Ąā ŌĀ v v‚āĀ) +‚Ąā (ŌĀ v v‚āā +‚Ąā ŌĀ v v‚āÉ)

infixl 6 _-‚Ąā_
_-‚Ąā_ : ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā ‚Üí ‚Ąā
a -‚Ąā b = a +‚Ąā (-‚Ąā b)

record K4Lattice' : Set where
  field
    num-cells : ‚Ąē
    cell-state : ‚Ąē ‚Üí K4State
    
lattice-total : K4Lattice' ‚Üí ‚Ąē
lattice-total lat = sum-cells (K4Lattice'.num-cells lat) 
  where
    sum-cells : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
    sum-cells zero = zero
    sum-cells (suc n) = total-amplitude (K4Lattice'.cell-state lat n) + sum-cells n

field-value : K4Lattice' ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
field-value lat i = total-amplitude (K4Lattice'.cell-state lat i)

record ThreeRoutesToK4 : Set where
  field
    -- ¬ß Route 1: Genesis chain produces 4 distinctions
    genesis-route       : GenesisBijection
    genesis-gives-4     : genesis-count ‚Č° 4

    -- ¬ß Route 2: Endomorphism classification has 4 cases
    endo-route          : (c : EndoCase) ‚Üí Fin4-to-EndoCase (EndoCase-to-Fin4 c) ‚Č° c

    -- ¬ß Route 3: Witness closure stabilises at 4
    witness-route       : K4WitnessLemma

    -- ¬ß Agreement: all three yield the same vertex count
    genesis-matches-K4  : genesis-count ‚Č° K4-V
    endo-matches-K4     : EndoCase-to-Fin4 case-dual ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))
    witness-matches-K4  : vertexCountK4 ‚Č° 4

  { genesis-route      = theorem-genesis-has-exactly-4
  ; genesis-gives-4    = theorem-genesis-count
  ; endo-route         = EndoCase-Fin4-roundtrip‚āĀ
  ; witness-route      = lemma-K4-witness
  ; genesis-matches-K4 = theorem-genesis-count
  ; endo-matches-K4    = refl
  ; witness-matches-K4 = refl
  }

genesis-pair-status = classify-pair

data SpacetimeIndex : Set where
  ŌĄ-idx : SpacetimeIndex
  x-idx : SpacetimeIndex
  y-idx : SpacetimeIndex
  z-idx : SpacetimeIndex

index-reversibility : SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí Reversibility
index-reversibility ŌĄ-idx = asymmetric
index-reversibility x-idx = symmetric
index-reversibility y-idx = symmetric
index-reversibility z-idx = symmetric

minkowskiSignature : SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
minkowskiSignature i j with i ‚Čü-idx j
  where
    _‚Čü-idx_ : SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí Bool
    ŌĄ-idx ‚Čü-idx ŌĄ-idx = true
    x-idx ‚Čü-idx x-idx = true
    y-idx ‚Čü-idx y-idx = true
    z-idx ‚Čü-idx z-idx = true
    _     ‚Čü-idx _     = false
... | false = 0‚Ą§
... | true  = signature-from-reversibility (index-reversibility i)

verify-ő∑-ŌĄŌĄ : minkowskiSignature ŌĄ-idx ŌĄ-idx ‚Č° -1‚Ą§
verify-ő∑-ŌĄŌĄ = refl

verify-ő∑-xx : minkowskiSignature x-idx x-idx ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
verify-ő∑-xx = refl

verify-ő∑-yy : minkowskiSignature y-idx y-idx ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
verify-ő∑-yy = refl

verify-ő∑-zz : minkowskiSignature z-idx z-idx ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
verify-ő∑-zz = refl

verify-ő∑-ŌĄx : minkowskiSignature ŌĄ-idx x-idx ‚Č° 0‚Ą§
verify-ő∑-ŌĄx = refl

signatureTrace : ‚Ą§
signatureTrace = ((minkowskiSignature ŌĄ-idx ŌĄ-idx +‚Ą§ 
                   minkowskiSignature x-idx x-idx) +‚Ą§
                   minkowskiSignature y-idx y-idx) +‚Ą§
                   minkowskiSignature z-idx z-idx

theorem-signature-trace : signatureTrace ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-signature-trace = refl

record FD-Emergence : Set where
  field
    step1-D‚āÄ          : Unavoidable Distinction
    step2-genesis     : genesis-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))
    step3-saturation  : K4MemorySaturation
    step4-D‚āÉ          : classify-pair D‚āÄ-id D‚āā-id ‚Č° new-irreducible
    
    step5-K‚āĄ          : k4-edge-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))
    step6-L-symmetric : ‚ąÄ (i j : K4Vertex) ‚Üí Laplacian i j ‚Č° Laplacian j i
    
    step7-eigenvector-1 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-1 őĽ‚āĄ
    step7-eigenvector-2 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-2 őĽ‚āĄ
    step7-eigenvector-3 : IsEigenvector eigenvector-3 őĽ‚āĄ
    
    step9-3D          : EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))

genesis-from-D‚āÄ : Unavoidable Distinction ‚Üí ‚Ąē
genesis-from-D‚āÄ _ = genesis-count

saturation-from-genesis : genesis-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc zero))) ‚Üí K4MemorySaturation
saturation-from-genesis refl = theorem-saturation

D‚āÉ-from-saturation : K4MemorySaturation ‚Üí classify-pair D‚āÄ-id D‚āā-id ‚Č° new-irreducible
D‚āÉ-from-saturation _ = theorem-D‚āÉ-emerges

K‚āĄ-from-D‚āÉ : classify-pair D‚āÄ-id D‚āā-id ‚Č° new-irreducible ‚Üí 
             k4-edge-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))
K‚āĄ-from-D‚āÉ _ = theorem-k4-has-6-edges

eigenvectors-from-K‚āĄ : k4-edge-count ‚Č° suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero))))) ‚Üí
  ((IsEigenvector eigenvector-1 őĽ‚āĄ) √ó (IsEigenvector eigenvector-2 őĽ‚āĄ)) √ó 
  (IsEigenvector eigenvector-3 őĽ‚āĄ)
eigenvectors-from-K‚āĄ _ = (theorem-eigenvector-1 , theorem-eigenvector-2) , theorem-eigenvector-3

dimension-from-eigenvectors : 
  ((IsEigenvector eigenvector-1 őĽ‚āĄ) √ó (IsEigenvector eigenvector-2 őĽ‚āĄ)) √ó 
  (IsEigenvector eigenvector-3 őĽ‚āĄ) ‚Üí EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))
dimension-from-eigenvectors _ = theorem-3D

theorem-D‚āÄ-to-3D : Unavoidable Distinction ‚Üí EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° suc (suc (suc zero))
theorem-D‚āÄ-to-3D unavoid = 
  let sat = saturation-from-genesis theorem-genesis-count
      d‚āÉ  = D‚āÉ-from-saturation sat
      k‚āĄ  = K‚āĄ-from-D‚āÉ d‚āÉ
      eig = eigenvectors-from-K‚āĄ k‚āĄ
  in dimension-from-eigenvectors eig

FD-proof : FD-Emergence
FD-proof = record
  { step1-D‚āÄ          = unavoidability-of-D‚āÄ
  ; step2-genesis     = theorem-genesis-count
  ; step3-saturation  = theorem-saturation
  ; step4-D‚āÉ          = theorem-D‚āÉ-emerges
  ; step5-K‚āĄ          = theorem-k4-has-6-edges
  ; step6-L-symmetric = theorem-L-symmetric
  ; step7-eigenvector-1 = theorem-eigenvector-1
  ; step7-eigenvector-2 = theorem-eigenvector-2
  ; step7-eigenvector-3 = theorem-eigenvector-3
  ; step9-3D          = theorem-3D
  }

SpectralPosition : Set
SpectralPosition = ‚Ą§ √ó (‚Ą§ √ó ‚Ą§)

spectralCoord : K4Vertex ‚Üí SpectralPosition
spectralCoord v = (eigenvector-1 v , (eigenvector-2 v , eigenvector-3 v))

pos-v‚āÄ : spectralCoord v‚āÄ ‚Č° (1‚Ą§ , (1‚Ą§ , 1‚Ą§))
pos-v‚āÄ = refl

pos-v‚āĀ : spectralCoord v‚āĀ ‚Č° (-1‚Ą§ , (0‚Ą§ , 0‚Ą§))

pos-v‚āā : spectralCoord v‚āā ‚Č° (0‚Ą§ , (-1‚Ą§ , 0‚Ą§))
pos-v‚āā = refl

pos-v‚āÉ : spectralCoord v‚āÉ ‚Č° (0‚Ą§ , (0‚Ą§ , -1‚Ą§))
pos-v‚āÉ = refl

sqDiff : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sqDiff a b = (a +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ b) *‚Ą§ (a +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ b)

distance¬≤ : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
distance¬≤ v w = 
  let (x‚āĀ , (y‚āĀ , z‚āĀ)) = spectralCoord v
      (x‚āā , (y‚āā , z‚āā)) = spectralCoord w
  in (sqDiff x‚āĀ x‚āā +‚Ą§ sqDiff y‚āĀ y‚āā) +‚Ą§ sqDiff z‚āĀ z‚āā

theorem-d01¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āÄ v‚āĀ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))) zero
theorem-d01¬≤ = refl

theorem-d02¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āÄ v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))) zero
theorem-d02¬≤ = refl

theorem-d03¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āÄ v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))) zero
theorem-d03¬≤ = refl

theorem-d12¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āĀ v‚āā ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-d12¬≤ = refl

theorem-d13¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āĀ v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-d13¬≤ = refl

theorem-d23¬≤ : distance¬≤ v‚āā v‚āÉ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ (suc (suc zero)) zero
theorem-d23¬≤ = refl

neighbors : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí Set
neighbors v n‚āĀ n‚āā n‚āÉ = (v ‚Č° v‚āÄ √ó (n‚āĀ ‚Č° v‚āĀ) √ó (n‚āā ‚Č° v‚āā) √ó (n‚āÉ ‚Č° v‚āÉ))

őĒx : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
őĒx v w = eigenvector-1 v +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (eigenvector-1 w)

őĒy : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
őĒy v w = eigenvector-2 v +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (eigenvector-2 w)

őĒz : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
őĒz v w = eigenvector-3 v +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (eigenvector-3 w)

metricComponent-xx : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
metricComponent-xx v‚āÄ = (sqDiff 1‚Ą§ -1‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ sqDiff 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§) +‚Ą§ sqDiff 1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
metricComponent-xx v‚āĀ = (sqDiff -1‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ sqDiff -1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§) +‚Ą§ sqDiff -1‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
metricComponent-xx v‚āā = (sqDiff 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ sqDiff 0‚Ą§ -1‚Ą§) +‚Ą§ sqDiff 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
metricComponent-xx v‚āÉ = (sqDiff 0‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ sqDiff 0‚Ą§ -1‚Ą§) +‚Ą§ sqDiff 0‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§


swap01 : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
swap01 v‚āÄ = v‚āĀ
swap01 v‚āĀ = v‚āÄ
swap01 v‚āā = v‚āā
swap01 v‚āÉ = v‚āÉ

graphDistance : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ąē
graphDistance v v' with vertex-to-id v | vertex-to-id v'
... | D‚āÄ-id | D‚āÄ-id = zero
... | D‚āĀ-id | D‚āĀ-id = zero
... | D‚āā-id | D‚āā-id = zero
... | D‚āÉ-id | D‚āÉ-id = zero
... | _   | _   = suc zero

theorem-K4-complete : ‚ąÄ (v w : K4Vertex) ‚Üí 
  (vertex-to-id v ‚Č° vertex-to-id w) ‚Üí graphDistance v w ‚Č° zero
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÄ v‚āÄ _ = refl
theorem-K4-complete v‚āĀ v‚āĀ _ = refl
theorem-K4-complete v‚āā v‚āā _ = refl
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÉ v‚āÉ _ = refl
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÄ v‚āĀ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÄ v‚āā ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÄ v‚āÉ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āĀ v‚āÄ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āĀ v‚āā ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āĀ v‚āÉ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āā v‚āÄ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āā v‚āĀ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āā v‚āÉ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÉ v‚āÄ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÉ v‚āĀ ()
theorem-K4-complete v‚āÉ v‚āā ()

d-from-eigenvalue-multiplicity : ‚Ąē
d-from-eigenvalue-multiplicity = K4-deg

d-from-eigenvector-count : ‚Ąē
d-from-eigenvector-count = K4-deg

d-from-V-minus-1 : ‚Ąē
d-from-V-minus-1 = K4-V ‚ął 1

d-from-spectral-gap : ‚Ąē
d-from-spectral-gap = K4-V ‚ął 1

record DimensionConsistency : Set where
  field
    from-multiplicity   : d-from-eigenvalue-multiplicity ‚Č° 3
    from-eigenvectors   : d-from-eigenvector-count ‚Č° 3
    from-V-minus-1      : d-from-V-minus-1 ‚Č° 3
    from-spectral-gap   : d-from-spectral-gap ‚Č° 3
    all-match           : EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° 3
    det-nonzero         : det-eigenvectors ‚Č° 1‚Ą§

theorem-d-consistency : DimensionConsistency
theorem-d-consistency = record
  { from-multiplicity   = refl
  ; from-eigenvectors   = refl
  ; from-V-minus-1      = refl
  ; from-spectral-gap   = refl
  ; all-match           = refl
  ; det-nonzero         = refl
  }

dimension-collapse : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 3
dimension-collapse n eq = trans (sym eq) theorem-3D

record MinkowskiStructure : Set where
  field
    one-asymmetric   : drift-asymmetric ‚Č° asymmetric
    three-symmetric  : k4-edge-symmetric ‚Č° symmetric
    spatial-count    : EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° 3
    trace-value      : signatureTrace ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ 2 zero

theorem-minkowski-structure : MinkowskiStructure
theorem-minkowski-structure = record
  { one-asymmetric = theorem-drift-unidirectional
  ; three-symmetric = refl
  ; spatial-count = theorem-3D
  ; trace-value = theorem-signature-trace
  }

DistinctionCount : Set
DistinctionCount = ‚Ąē

genesis-state : DistinctionCount
genesis-state = suc (suc (suc zero))

k4-state : DistinctionCount
k4-state = suc genesis-state


-- ¬ß K4-SPECTRAL

record DimensionExclusivity : Set where
  field
    collapse-to-3            : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° n ‚Üí n ‚Č° 3
    primary-forcing          : d-from-V-minus-1 ‚Č° EmbeddingDimension
    eigenspace-confirms      : count-őĽ‚āĄ-eigenvectors ‚Č° EmbeddingDimension
    candidate-2-eliminated   : ¬¨ (EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° 2)
    candidate-4-eliminated   : ¬¨ (EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° 4)
    K4-gives-3D              : EmbeddingDimension ‚Č° 3

theorem-d-exclusivity : DimensionExclusivity
theorem-d-exclusivity = record
  { collapse-to-3 = dimension-collapse
  ; primary-forcing = refl
  ; eigenspace-confirms = theorem-eigenspace-determines-dimension
  ; candidate-2-eliminated = dimension-not-2
  ; candidate-4-eliminated = dimension-not-4
  ; K4-gives-3D  = refl
  }

record TimeConsistency : Set where
  field
    from-K4-structure     : time-dimensions ‚Č° (K4-V ‚ął EmbeddingDimension)
    from-spacetime-split  : t-from-spacetime-split ‚Č° 1
    both-give-1           : time-dimensions ‚Č° 1
    splits-match          : time-dimensions ‚Č° t-from-spacetime-split

theorem-t-consistency : TimeConsistency
theorem-t-consistency = record
  { from-K4-structure    = refl
  ; from-spacetime-split = refl
  ; both-give-1          = refl
  ; splits-match         = refl
  }

record TimeExclusivity : Set where
  field
    not-0D         : ¬¨ (time-dimensions ‚Č° 0)
    not-2D         : ¬¨ (time-dimensions ‚Č° 2)
    exactly-1D     : time-dimensions ‚Č° 1
    signature-3-1  : EmbeddingDimension + time-dimensions ‚Č° 4

lemma-1-not-0 : ¬¨ (1 ‚Č° 0)
lemma-1-not-0 ()

lemma-1-not-2 : ¬¨ (1 ‚Č° 2)
lemma-1-not-2 ()

theorem-t-exclusivity : TimeExclusivity
theorem-t-exclusivity = record
  { not-0D         = lemma-1-not-0
  ; not-2D         = lemma-1-not-2
  ; exactly-1D     = refl
  ; signature-3-1  = refl
  }

kappa-if-t-equals-0 : ‚Ąē
kappa-if-t-equals-0 = 2 * (EmbeddingDimension + 0)

kappa-if-t-equals-2 : ‚Ąē
kappa-if-t-equals-2 = 2 * (EmbeddingDimension + 2)

kappa-with-correct-t : ‚Ąē
kappa-with-correct-t = 2 * (EmbeddingDimension + time-dimensions)


-- ¬ß FOUNDATION

data PairKnown : DistinctionCount ‚Üí Set where
  genesis-knows-D‚āÄD‚āĀ : PairKnown genesis-state
  
  k4-knows-D‚āÄD‚āĀ : PairKnown k4-state
  k4-knows-D‚āÄD‚āā : PairKnown k4-state

pairs-known : DistinctionCount ‚Üí ‚Ąē
pairs-known zero = zero
pairs-known (suc zero) = zero
pairs-known (suc (suc zero)) = suc zero
pairs-known (suc (suc (suc zero))) = suc zero
pairs-known (suc (suc (suc (suc n)))) = suc (suc zero)


-- ¬ß SPACETIME

  field
    t0-breaks-kappa   : ¬¨ (kappa-if-t-equals-0 ‚Č° 8)
    t2-breaks-kappa   : ¬¨ (kappa-if-t-equals-2 ‚Č° 8)
    t1-gives-kappa-8  : kappa-with-correct-t ‚Č° 8
    causality-needs-1 : time-dimensions ‚Č° 1

lemma-6-not-8'' : ¬¨ (6 ‚Č° 8)
lemma-6-not-8'' ()

lemma-10-not-8' : ¬¨ (10 ‚Č° 8)
lemma-10-not-8' ()

theorem-t-robustness = record
  { t0-breaks-kappa   = lemma-6-not-8''
  ; t2-breaks-kappa   = lemma-10-not-8'
  ; t1-gives-kappa-8  = refl
  ; causality-needs-1 = refl
  }

spacetime-dimension = EmbeddingDimension + time-dimensions

-- ¬ß Group operation: function composition on K4Vertex
infixr 20 _‚ąė‚āĖ_
_‚ąė‚āĖ_ : (K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex) ‚Üí (K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex) ‚Üí (K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex)
(f ‚ąė‚āĖ g) v = f (g v)

-- ¬ß The identity permutation
id‚āĖ : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
id‚āĖ v = v

-- ¬ß (01): swap v‚āÄ ‚ÜĒ v‚āĀ
ŌĄ01 : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
ŌĄ01 v‚āÄ = v‚āĀ
ŌĄ01 v‚āĀ = v‚āÄ
ŌĄ01 v‚āā = v‚āā
ŌĄ01 v‚āÉ = v‚āÉ

-- ¬ß (02): swap v‚āÄ ‚ÜĒ v‚āā
ŌĄ02 : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
ŌĄ02 v‚āÄ = v‚āā
ŌĄ02 v‚āā = v‚āÄ
ŌĄ02 v‚āĀ = v‚āĀ
ŌĄ02 v‚āÉ = v‚āÉ

-- ¬ß (03): swap v‚āÄ ‚ÜĒ v‚āÉ
ŌĄ03 : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
ŌĄ03 v‚āÄ = v‚āÉ
ŌĄ03 v‚āÉ = v‚āÄ
ŌĄ03 v‚āĀ = v‚āĀ
ŌĄ03 v‚āā = v‚āā

-- ¬ß (12): swap v‚āĀ ‚ÜĒ v‚āā
ŌĄ12 : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex
ŌĄ12 v‚āĀ = v‚āā
ŌĄ12 v‚āā = v‚āĀ
ŌĄ12 v‚āÄ = v‚āÄ
ŌĄ12 v‚āÉ = v‚āÉ

ŌĄ13 v‚āÉ = v‚āĀ
ŌĄ13 v‚āÄ = v‚āÄ
ŌĄ13 v‚āā = v‚āā

ŌÉ-0231 v‚āā = v‚āĀ

-- ¬ß SU(n) generators = n¬≤ - 1
-- ¬ß The quotient orders give the n in SU(n)
SU-dim-from-quotient : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
SU-dim-from-quotient n = n * n ‚ął 1

-- ¬ß Z‚āÉ quotient ‚Üí SU(3) with 3¬≤-1 = 8 generators

-- ¬ß A 4-vector over ‚Ą§
S4Vec : Set
S4Vec = K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§

-- ¬ß Permutation action: ŌÉ acts on a vector by permuting indices
perm-act : (K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex) ‚Üí S4Vec ‚Üí S4Vec
perm-act ŌÉ x v = x (ŌÉ v)

-- ¬ß The constant vector (1,1,1,1)
ones-vec : S4Vec
ones-vec _ = 1‚Ą§

-- ¬ß Sum of components
vec-sum : S4Vec ‚Üí ‚Ą§
vec-sum x = (x v‚āÄ +‚Ą§ x v‚āĀ) +‚Ą§ (x v‚āā +‚Ą§ x v‚āÉ)

theorem-ones-invariant-ŌĄ01 : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí perm-act ŌĄ01 ones-vec v ‚Č° ones-vec v
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌĄ01 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌĄ01 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌĄ01 v‚āā = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌĄ01 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-ones-invariant-cyc012 : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí perm-act cyc012 ones-vec v ‚Č° ones-vec v
theorem-ones-invariant-cyc012 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-cyc012 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-cyc012 v‚āā = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-cyc012 v‚āÉ = refl

theorem-ones-invariant-ŌÉ0123 : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí perm-act ŌÉ-0123 ones-vec v ‚Č° ones-vec v
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌÉ0123 v‚āÄ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌÉ0123 v‚āĀ = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌÉ0123 v‚āā = refl
theorem-ones-invariant-ŌÉ0123 v‚āÉ = refl

-- ¬ß V‚āÉ membership: sum of components is zero (propositional equality on ‚Ą§)
is-in-V‚āÉ : S4Vec ‚Üí Set
is-in-V‚āÉ x = vec-sum x ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§

-- ¬ß Three basis vectors of V‚āÉ
-- ¬ß e‚āĀ - e‚āÄ = (-1, 1, 0, 0)
v‚āÉ-basis-1 : S4Vec
-- ¬ß -1 in our ‚Ą§ representation
v‚āÉ-basis-1 v‚āÄ = mk‚Ą§ 0 1
v‚āÉ-basis-1 v‚āĀ = 1‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-1 v‚āā = 0‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-1 v‚āÉ = 0‚Ą§

-- ¬ß e‚āā - e‚āÄ = (-1, 0, 1, 0)
v‚āÉ-basis-2 : S4Vec
v‚āÉ-basis-2 v‚āÄ = mk‚Ą§ 0 1
v‚āÉ-basis-2 v‚āĀ = 0‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-2 v‚āā = 1‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-2 v‚āÉ = 0‚Ą§

-- ¬ß e‚āÉ - e‚āÄ = (-1, 0, 0, 1)
v‚āÉ-basis-3 : S4Vec
v‚āÉ-basis-3 v‚āÄ = mk‚Ą§ 0 1
v‚āÉ-basis-3 v‚āĀ = 0‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-3 v‚āā = 0‚Ą§
v‚āÉ-basis-3 v‚āÉ = 1‚Ą§

theorem-basis1-in-V‚āÉ : vec-sum v‚āÉ-basis-1 ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-basis1-in-V‚āÉ = refl

theorem-basis2-in-V‚āÉ : vec-sum v‚āÉ-basis-2 ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-basis2-in-V‚āÉ = refl

theorem-basis3-in-V‚āÉ : vec-sum v‚āÉ-basis-3 ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-basis3-in-V‚āÉ = refl

-- ¬ß Permutations preserve zero-sum
theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-őīx : vec-sum (perm-act őī-x v‚āÉ-basis-1) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-őīx = refl

theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-cyc012 : vec-sum (perm-act cyc012 v‚āÉ-basis-1) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-cyc012 = refl

theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 : vec-sum (perm-act ŌĄ01 v‚āÉ-basis-1) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-perm-preserves-V‚āÉ-ŌĄ01 = refl

record StandardRepresentation : Set where
  field
    -- ¬ß Matrices are in GL(3,‚Ą§): determinant is ¬Ī1
    ŌĄ01-odd      : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-ŌĄ01    ‚Č° neg‚Ą§ 1‚Ą§
    cyc012-even  : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-cyc012 ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
    -- ¬ß The three V‚āĄ generators have determinant +1 (even permutations)
    őīx-even      : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīx     ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
    őīy-even      : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīy     ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
    őīz-even      : det3 ŌĀ‚āÉ-őīz     ‚Č° 1‚Ą§
    -- ¬ß Identity has determinant 1
    id-det       : det3 I‚āÉ‚Ą§       ‚Č° 1‚Ą§

theorem-ŌĀ‚āÉ-representation : StandardRepresentation
theorem-ŌĀ‚āÉ-representation = record
  { ŌĄ01-odd     = refl
  ; cyc012-even = refl
  ; őīx-even     = refl
  ; őīy-even     = refl
  ; őīz-even     = refl
  ; id-det      = refl
  }

-- ¬ß The eigenvalue-4 eigenvectors are in V‚āÉ
-- ¬ß Recall from spectral theory: eigenvectors are 
-- ¬ß w‚āĀ = (-1, 1, 0, 0), w‚āā = (-1, 0, 1, 0), w‚āÉ = (-1, 0, 0, 1)
-- ¬ß These are exactly v‚āÉ-basis-1, v‚āÉ-basis-2, v‚āÉ-basis-3

theorem-spectral-rep-coincide-1 : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí v‚āÉ-basis-1 v ‚Č° v‚āÉ-basis-1 v
theorem-spectral-rep-coincide-1 _ = refl

-- ¬ß The representation dimension equals the eigenspace multiplicity

record SpectralRepresentationCoincidence : Set where
  field
    eigenspace-dim : ‚Ąē
    rep-dim        : ‚Ąē
    dims-agree     : eigenspace-dim ‚Č° rep-dim
    both-are-3     : eigenspace-dim ‚Č° 3
    basis-in-V‚āÉ    : vec-sum v‚āÉ-basis-1 ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§

theorem-spectral-rep : SpectralRepresentationCoincidence
theorem-spectral-rep = record
  { eigenspace-dim = 3
  ; rep-dim        = degree-K4
  ; dims-agree     = refl
  ; both-are-3     = refl
  ; basis-in-V‚āÉ    = refl
  }

theorem-metric-uniform v‚āÉ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = refl
theorem-metric-uniform v‚āÉ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = refl
theorem-metric-uniform v‚āÉ v‚āā őľ őĹ = refl
theorem-metric-uniform v‚āÉ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = refl

metricDeriv-computed : K4Vertex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
metricDeriv-computed v w őľ őĹ = metricK4 w őľ őĹ +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (metricK4 v őľ őĹ)

metricK4-diff-zero : ‚ąÄ (v w : K4Vertex) (őľ őĹ : SpacetimeIndex) ‚Üí
  (metricK4 w őľ őĹ +‚Ą§ neg‚Ą§ (metricK4 v őľ őĹ)) ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÄ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÄ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÄ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÄ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÄ v‚āā őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÄ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÄ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÄ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āĀ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āĀ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āĀ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āĀ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āĀ v‚āā őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āĀ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āĀ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āĀ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āā v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āā őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āā v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āā őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āā v‚āā őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āā őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āā v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āā őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÉ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÉ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÉ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÉ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÉ v‚āā őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÉ őľ őĹ)
metricK4-diff-zero v‚āÉ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v‚āÉ őľ őĹ)

theorem-metricDeriv-vanishes : ‚ąÄ (v w : K4Vertex) (őľ őĹ : SpacetimeIndex) ‚Üí
                                metricDeriv-computed v w őľ őĹ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-metricDeriv-vanishes = metricK4-diff-zero

metricDeriv : SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí K4Vertex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
metricDeriv őĽ' v őľ őĹ = metricDeriv-computed v v őľ őĹ

theorem-metric-deriv-vanishes : ‚ąÄ (őĽ' : SpacetimeIndex) (v : K4Vertex) 
                                  (őľ őĹ : SpacetimeIndex) ‚Üí
                                metricDeriv őĽ' v őľ őĹ ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§
theorem-metric-deriv-vanishes őĽ' v őľ őĹ = +‚Ą§-inverse ≥ (metricK4 v őľ őĹ)

metricK4-truly-uniform : ‚ąÄ (v w : K4Vertex) (őľ őĹ : SpacetimeIndex) ‚Üí
  metricK4 v őľ őĹ ‚Č° metricK4 w őľ őĹ
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āÄ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āÄ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āÄ v‚āā őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āÄ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = refl

metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āĀ v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = refl

metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āĀ v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = refl

metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āā v‚āĀ őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āā v‚āā őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āā v‚āÉ őľ őĹ = refl
metricK4-truly-uniform v‚āÉ v‚āÄ őľ őĹ = refl

theorem-metric-diagonal : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí metricK4 v ŌĄ-idx x-idx ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ 0‚Ą§

spectralRicci : K4Vertex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
spectralRicci v ŌĄ-idx ŌĄ-idx = 0‚Ą§
spectralRicci v x-idx x-idx = őĽ‚āĄ
spectralRicci v y-idx y-idx = őĽ‚āĄ
spectralRicci v z-idx z-idx = őĽ‚āĄ
spectralRicci v _     _     = 0‚Ą§

spectralRicciScalar : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
spectralRicciScalar v = (spectralRicci v x-idx x-idx +‚Ą§
                         spectralRicci v y-idx y-idx) +‚Ą§
                         spectralRicci v z-idx z-idx

twelve : ‚Ąē
twelve = suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))))))))

three : ‚Ąē
three = suc (suc (suc zero))

theorem-spectral-ricci-scalar : ‚ąÄ (v : K4Vertex) ‚Üí 
  spectralRicciScalar v ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ twelve zero
theorem-spectral-ricci-scalar v = refl

cosmologicalConstant : ‚Ą§
cosmologicalConstant = mk‚Ą§ three zero

theorem-lambda-from-K4 : cosmologicalConstant ‚ČÉ‚Ą§ mk‚Ą§ three zero
theorem-lambda-from-K4 = refl

lambdaTerm : K4Vertex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
lambdaTerm v őľ őĹ = cosmologicalConstant *‚Ą§ metricK4 v őľ őĹ

geometricRicci : K4Vertex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí SpacetimeIndex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
geometricRicci v őľ őĹ = 0‚Ą§

geometricRicciScalar : K4Vertex ‚Üí ‚Ą§
